{"name":"Soulpulse Resonance System — Production Canon v1.0","type":"document","content":"# Soulpulse Resonance System — Production Canon v1.0\n\n**Purpose:** Lock final, production-ready rules for on-page use of Soulpulse across all books/episodes. This is the baseline for consistency, training new writers, and catching drift.\n\n---\n\n## 0) TL;DR — The Three-Line Rule\n1) **It’s resonance, not force.** Effects arise by **attuning** the user’s pulse to the target’s natural frequency.\n2) **Costs are mandatory and visible.** **Vein-burn → echo → fatigue/identity tax** track on-page. Hollowing is irreversible.\n3) **Four principles, two axes, one paradox:** **Form ↔ Entropy**, **Purity ↔ Wholeness**. **Confluence** = all four at once; terminal for mortals.\n\n---\n\n## 1) Metaphysics\n- **World substrate:** A planetary vein-network carries vibrational energy (\"Soulpulse\"). Every material/life-form has a **natural frequency** (NF).\n- **User substrate:** A practitioner’s **soul-frequency** can be modulated via breath, intent, gesture, and tools to match a target’s NF (= **attunement**). \n- **Fields:** Use creates a **pulse-field** (PF) that propagates through local matter and interacts with other PFs (constructive/destructive interference). \n- **Opposition:** Invoking one principle automatically rouses resistance from its opposite. No stable “pure” state exists without a counterforce.\n\n### The Four Principles (operational view)\n- **Form (Structure):** impose/restore ideal geometry; reinforce, lock, crystallize; long-lived constructs that still decay over time.\n- **Wholeness (Continuity):** knit, link, mend; empathic bridges; stabilize flows; limited cross-material bonding.\n- **Purity (Cleansing):** separate, refine, excise; selective burn; judgment-directional and prone to collateral when over-driven.\n- **Entropy (Dissolution):** release, end, soften bonds; accelerate decay; nullify constructs and soothe endings.\n\n**Divine opposition pairs:** Form⇄Entropy, Purity⇄Wholeness.\n\n---\n\n## 2) Core Mechanics & Safe Ops\n\n### 2.1 Attunement Protocol (single-user)\n**Goal:** establish resonance match with the smallest harmful delta.\n1) **Probe:** low-amplitude pulse pings; read tactile/auditory/empathic feedback.\n2) **Trim:** micro-adjust breath tempo and focus; bring buzz → hum.\n3) **Seat:** hold steady 2–8 breaths to stabilize.\n4) **Work:** scale amplitude gradually while monitoring PF stability.\n5) **Damp:** active cooldown (grounding, breath reset) to clear **vein-echo**.\n\n*Failure heuristic:* push-through on mismatch = **dissonance → vein-burn → snap**.\n\n### 2.2 Multi-Resonance / “Overtones”\n- **Two-tone (dual):** rare, trainable in exceptional users; sharply increases strain. Treat as **hazard class Beta**.\n- **Chord (3–4):** unstable; mortals cannot hold safely outside split-second flares.\n- **Confluence (all four simultaneous):** **paradox engine.** Mortals: **terminal**. Gods: not achievable (each is a pure aspect). \n\n### 2.3 Pulse-Field Dynamics\n- **Echo Stacking:** residual PF lingers after use; back-to-back workings amplify error. Writers must include either **wait** or **damp** step.\n- **Resonance Cascade:** uncontrolled propagation via substrate (structures/veins) causing chain failures, quakes, or collapses.\n- **Team Interference:** uncoordinated PFs create feedback. **Stagger** or **choir** (see §2.4) to avoid.\n\n### 2.4 Group Work — Choir & Ring Patterns\n- **Duo Harmonic:** lead sets NF; partner rides the overtone. Use for complex repairs or combat shielding.\n- **Fivefold Choir (healing):** staggered entries, overlapping 2-breath windows; one **breaker** assigned to cut links on overload.\n- **Structural Ring (8–12):** equidistant placement; rotate leads every 3–5 breaths; **anchor** maintains phase clock.\n\n---\n\n## 3) Costs, Injuries, and Failure Modes\n\n### 3.1 Mandatory Costs (choose ≥1 per working on-page)\n- **Physio:** tremor, after-heat, joint stiffness (principle-specific manifestations).\n- **Psycho:** empathy bleed (Wholeness), perfection fixation (Form), zealotry/isolation (Purity), fatigue/nihilism (Entropy).\n- **Systemic:** rising **vein-burn** level; visible channel glow/scar progression.\n\n### 3.2 Progressive Injury Ladder\n1) **After-heat / sting** → rest resolves.\n2) **Vein-burn** (micro-tears, glow) → requires cooldown & care.\n3) **Vein-snap** (channel rupture) → collapse, localized loss of function.\n4) **Hollowing** (conviction failure; resonance goes dark) → **irreversible**.\n\n### 3.3 Link-Specific Hazards\n- **Sympathetic Overload:** healer shares target’s pain/trauma; requires **breaker**.\n- **Identity Bleed:** blurred self/other after repeated Wholeness.\n- **Over-Purity:** auto-immolating burn; collateral via over-selection.\n- **Over-Form:** calcification/ossification; cognitive rigidity.\n- **Over-Entropy:** dissociation, premature aging signatures.\n\n---\n\n## 4) Combat & Field Applications\n\n### 4.1 Techniques (legal for protagonists)\n- **Tethering:** latch onto opponent NF to damp/enhance. High-risk; establish cutout.\n- **Null Pulse (Entropy):** quick dissolve of enemy constructs or ongoing PFs.\n- **Lattice Salves:** prep items that resonate on activation as low-amplitude aids.\n- **Pop-up Forts (Form):** short-duration girders/plates; require renewal; expect Purity/Entropy counters.\n- **Choir Shields (Wholeness):** rotating duty; explicit strain tracking.\n\n### 4.2 Counters & Anti-magic\n- **Suppression Fields:** dissonant blankets that jam PFs; risk of systemic **Cascade** if scaled wide on stressed networks.\n- **On-page response:** narrow bandwidth, local dampers, or **go silent** (no PF) until field cycles.\n\n---\n\n## 5) Quantitative Dials (for scene design)\n- **Pulse classes:** Micro (tool aid) / Standard (scene beat) / Grand (set-piece). \n- **Breath economy:** Most safe workings resolve in **2–8 breaths**. Anything >12 breaths must show multiple costs.\n- **Cooldown:** Minimum **1–3 breaths** quiet after micro; **dozens** after grand; choir requires rotation.\n- **Range:** Direct-contact is safest; line-of-sight possible with increased error; long-range via substrates invites Cascade.\n\n---\n\n## 6) Canon-by-Principle (writer crib)\n\n### Form\n- **Essence:** order/geometry/reinforcement. \n- **Signatures:** crystalline hum, blue-silver glow, rigidity metaphors.\n- **Costs:** stiffness, calcification, rule-obsession. \n- **Antagonisms:** undone by Entropy pulses; brittle under Purity over-selection.\n\n### Wholeness\n- **Essence:** mending/linking/stabilizing flows.\n- **Signatures:** warm hum, copper-gold light, shared sensation.\n- **Costs:** fatigue, identity bleed, sympathetic overload risk.\n- **Antagonisms:** severed by Purity; destabilized by heavy Form reconfiguration.\n\n### Purity\n- **Essence:** excision/refinement/absolution.\n- **Signatures:** white glare, selective burn, narrowing focus.\n- **Costs:** inflammation, isolation, zeal escalation; risk auto-immolation at extremes.\n- **Antagonisms:** blunted by Wholeness links; rigid Form traps can redirect Purity blasts.\n\n### Entropy\n- **Essence:** release/ending/softening bonds.\n- **Signatures:** gray hush, wither/flake, easing.\n- **Costs:** vitality drain, chill, melancholy, detachment.\n- **Antagonisms:** resisted by fresh Form reinforcements; Purity can “burn through” rot if absolutely directed.\n\n---\n\n## 7) Confluence & Endgame Constraints\n- **Definition:** full simultaneous resonance of all four principles.\n- **Rules:**\n  - Mortals: **terminal** (veins calcify/burn out; self-sacrificial window only).\n  - Gods: **cannot** Confluence (each is a pure aspect, not a chord).\n  - **Stasis constructs** created by Confluence (e.g., fivefold cages) trap; kills require **external teams**.\n- **On-page:** display escalating **vein-burn clock**, sensory overload, and macro-environmental hum at distance.\n\n---\n\n## 8) Scene Execution Checklist (drop-in)\n**Before:**\n- Establish target NF cues (sound/texture/heat/feel). \n- Name principle(s) intended. \n- Define success state and **one** hard limit.\n\n**During:**\n- Show probe → trim → seat → work. \n- Log costs (physio/psycho/systemic). \n- Manage echo (pause/damp) or choir rotation.\n\n**After:**\n- Show world “ringing” or settling. \n- Update **vein-burn meter** for the user. \n- If group, name the **breaker** status.\n\n---\n\n## 9) Exploit Prevention & Edge Cases\n- **No free heals:** Wholeness always trades something (time, pain, fatigue, identity tax).\n- **No infinite walls:** Form constructs require renewal; entropy gnaws; Purity and Entropy have clean counters.\n- **Purity selectivity cap:** cannot excise beyond user’s discrimination bandwidth; stress widens the cut and raises collateral.\n- **Entropy precision:** small, surgical dissolves require calm and practice; panic spreads the rot.\n- **Echo discipline:** stacking different principles without damp multiplies dissonance; order your chord deliberately.\n\n---\n\n## 10) Glossary (ops terms)\n- **Attunement:** matching one’s pulse to target NF.\n- **Pulse-Field (PF):** temporary resonance aura created by use.\n- **Vein-echo:** residual vibration in user/environment post-use.\n- **Dissonance:** mismatch between pulses → pain/damage/chaos.\n- **Vein-burn / Vein-snap:** graded channel injuries (scar vs rupture).\n- **Hollowing:** catastrophic conviction failure; permanent.\n- **Overtone:** secondary principle layered atop the primary.\n- **Breaker:** teammate assigned to sever dangerous links.\n- **Choir/Ring:** coordinated group patterns for healing/structure.\n- **Tethering:** latching onto another’s NF to modulate it.\n\n---\n\n## 11) Writer Notes & Style\n- Use in-world craft verbs: **true, seat, brace, purge, knit, release**. Avoid “cast spell.”\n- Track **breaths** and **burn** like stamina bars; make costs legible.\n- Echo the **domain aesthetics** in sensory description (geometry/white fire/gold warmth/gray hush).\n\n---\n\n### Change Log\n- v1.0 — Initial consolidation for room circulation.\n"}

# SOULPULSE MAGIC SYSTEM REFERENCE — N05 SCOPE
## "Steal Breaks Open" — Confluence Manifests, Gods Awaken

---

## KNOWLEDGE BOUNDARY

**What characters know by end of N05:**
- **Four Principles formalized** (Form, Wholeness, Purity, Entropy)
- **Confluence discovered** (all four principles simultaneously—Jhace only)
- **Suppression technology** exists and catastrophically failed
- **God-vessel transformations** completed (four individuals became gods)
- **Vein network theory** understood through catastrophe
- **Complete Soulpulse framework** established

**This is the culmination:** All major magic system discoveries complete by N05 end.

---

## PART 1: FOUR PRINCIPLES (Formalized Framework)

### **Complete Theoretical Understanding:**

**By N05, practitioners understand:**
- Four fundamental principles govern Soulpulse
- Each principle represents aspect of reality
- All matter/energy resonates with one or more principles
- Practitioners align with principle matching conviction
- Multi-principle mastery possible but extremely rare
- Confluence (all four) thought impossible until Jhace

---

### **1. FORM (Structural Principle)**

**Essence:** Geometric order, precision, rigidity
**Frequency:** High crystalline
**Materials:** Inorganic (metal, glass, stone)
**Glow:** Blue-silver, angular patterns
**Sound:** High-pitched chime, crystalline ringing
**Sensation:** Cool, sharp, precise

**What It Does:**
- Shapes materials with precision
- Stabilizes structures
- Creates geometric barriers
- Locks forms in place
- Enforces order

**Physical Cost:**
- Calcification (joints hardening)
- Mental exhaustion from precision
- Coldness in extremities
- Tremors from sustained use

**God-Vessel:** Corlexi → Xilcore (Form Incarnate)

---

### **2. WHOLENESS (Continuity Principle)**

**Essence:** Connection, healing, flow
**Frequency:** Mid-range warmth
**Materials:** Organic, bonds, connections
**Glow:** Copper-gold, flowing patterns
**Sound:** Mid-range hum, harmonic overtones
**Sensation:** Warm, flowing, connecting

**What It Does:**
- Heals wounds
- Mends connections
- Maintains continuity
- Bonds disparate elements
- Preserves wholeness

**Physical Cost:**
- Vein-burn (copper-gold marks growing)
- Identity bleed (feeling others)
- Deep exhaustion
- Sympathetic overload risk

**God-Vessel:** Salee → Leesa (Wholeness Incarnate)

---

### **3. PURITY (Sanctification Principle)**

**Essence:** Separation, cleansing, judgment
**Frequency:** Piercing, clear
**Materials:** Purification, burning
**Glow:** White-gold, blinding
**Sound:** Single piercing tone
**Sensation:** Burning, separating, painful

**What It Does:**
- Cleanses contamination
- Separates pure from impure
- Burns away corruption
- Creates sterile fields
- Enforces purity

**Physical Cost:**
- Tissue swelling (hands, joints)
- Isolation tendency (emotional numbness)
- Pain during use
- Physical sensitivity

**God-Vessel:** Mobel → Blemo (Purity Incarnate)

---

### **4. ENTROPY (Dissolution Principle)**

**Essence:** Endings, decay, acceptance
**Frequency:** Low, soft, fading
**Materials:** Dissolution, controlled decay
**Glow:** Ash-gray, dispersing
**Sound:** Low soft hum, fading tones
**Sensation:** Cool release, peaceful surrender

**What It Does:**
- Accelerates natural decay
- Facilitates peaceful endings
- Controlled dissolution
- Acceptance of inevitable
- Gentle release

**Physical Cost:**
- Vitality drain (aging effect)
- Fatalism intensifies
- Physical weakness
- Existential exhaustion

**God-Vessel:** Eries → Seeri (Entropy Incarnate)

---

## PART 2: CONFLUENCE (Jhace's Discovery)

### **What It Is:**

**Definition:**
Ability to wield all four Soulpulse principles simultaneously. Previously thought impossible. Only known practitioner: Jhace Torrins.

**Why Thought Impossible:**
- Four frequencies contradictory (order vs. chaos, connection vs. separation)
- Mental focus can't split four ways
- Physical cost of one principle already severe
- Combining four should cause immediate Hollowing
- No theoretical framework suggested possibility

---

### **How Jhace Manifested It (N05 Ch13)**

**Context:**
- Tiffani died shielding him from debris
- Overwhelming grief + desperate need to save others
- Suppression device failing catastrophically
- Reality destabilizing around him

**The Moment:**
- Instinctive, not deliberate
- Driven by love, grief, need
- All four principles erupted simultaneously
- Blinding explosion of all four glows at once
- Combined with suppression device failure
- Massive energy discharge

**What It Looked Like:**
- Blue-silver (Form) + Copper-gold (Wholeness) + White-gold (Purity) + Ash-gray (Entropy) simultaneously
- Geometric patterns + organic flow + purifying flame + peaceful dissolution
- All four frequencies harmonizing impossibly
- Reality warping, reshaping, stabilizing, dissolving at once

**Effect:**
- Saved survivors in immediate area
- Triggered four god-vessel transformations simultaneously
- Ended vein-shatter earthquakes permanently
- Broke part of Te'Oga's crust free
- Thousands died from energy wave
- World irrevocably transformed

**Why Jhace Could Do It:**
- Natural multi-affinity (like Chloen)
- Years of instinctive multi-principle work (unrecognized)
- Deep conviction in all four principles simultaneously
- Grief provided catalyst
- Love for Tiffani transcended contradictions
- Unique psychological/spiritual state

---

### **Jhace's Confluence Capabilities (Post-N05)**

**What He Can Do:**
- Use all four principles
- Switch between them fluidly
- Combine two or more (various combinations)
- Theoretical maximum: all four simultaneously (only done once, during Tiffani's death)

**Limitations:**
- Each use still costs
- Combining principles multiplies cost
- Full Confluence (all four) nearly killed him
- Unlikely to use full Confluence again (trauma-associated)
- Prefers using principles singly or in pairs

**Significance:**
- Only human capable of opposing gods
- Bridge between all four factions
- Living proof principles can harmonize
- Unique position in post-transformation world

---

## PART 3: SUPPRESSION TECHNOLOGY

### **What It Is:**

**Sanitist Suppression Device:**
Technology deployed by anti-magic authorities to dampen all Soulpulse activity. Intended to calm magic, prevent violence, protect people from resonance danger.

**How It Was Supposed to Work:**
- Generate counter-frequency field
- Dampen all Soulpulse activity in area
- Reduce resonance to safe levels
- Temporary effect, no permanent damage

**Why It Failed Catastrophically:**

**"Steal Breaks Open" Effect:**
- Suppression created pressure on vein network
- Like damming river without outlet
- Built-up energy had nowhere to go
- When device failed, all suppressed energy erupted at once
- Catastrophic chain reaction

**What Actually Happened:**
1. Device activated during battle (N05 Ch11)
2. Suppressed all Soulpulse activity
3. Energy built up in planetary vein network
4. Pressure exceeded tolerances
5. Vein network broke open
6. Massive uncontrolled discharge
7. Combined with Jhace's Confluence
8. Four god-vessels awakened simultaneously
9. Part of Te'Oga's crust broke free
10. Thousands died, world transformed

---

### **Vein Network (Finally Understood)**

**What It Is:**
Invisible planetary network of energy channels. Like veins in living organism. Carries Soulpulse energy throughout Te'Oga.

**Discovery:**
- Theoretical before Piercing
- Activated by Piercing impact
- Became responsive to human will
- Suppression device failure made network visible/obvious
- Complete understanding only post-catastrophe

**Characteristics:**
- Responds to resonance frequency
- Channels energy through planet
- Can be damaged (vein-snap)
- Can cascade failures
- Breaking open = catastrophic discharge

**Post-Steal Breaks Open:**
- Chronic vein-shatter earthquakes ceased
- Network stabilized at new equilibrium
- Permanently altered by god-vessel transformations
- Now obviously interconnected with gods

---

## PART 4: GOD-VESSEL TRANSFORMATIONS

### **The Four (Completed N05 Ch13)**

**1. CORLEXI → XILCORE (Form)**
- **Location:** Prism city (recovering from Hollowing)
- **Transformation:** Energy wave restructured body into geometric perfection
- **First Act:** Reassembled structures into flawless forms
- **Domain:** Geometric perfection, law, order
- **Following:** Craftsmen, architects, soldiers seeking discipline

**2. SALEE → LEESA (Wholeness)**
- **Location:** Cauldron-Hold medical center
- **Transformation:** Absorbed all patient pain, became living mercy
- **First Act:** Healed dozens simultaneously
- **Domain:** Compassion, healing, connection
- **Following:** Those she saved, healers, community organizers

**3. MOBEL → BLEMO (Purity)**
- **Location:** Eastern territories (battle site)
- **Transformation:** Incinerating purification, violent emergence
- **First Act:** Separated pure from impure with clear division
- **Domain:** Purity, judgment, separation
- **Following:** Radical devotees, zealots, purists

**4. ERIES → SEERI (Entropy)**
- **Location:** Isolated caves
- **Transformation:** Serene dissolution, peaceful emergence
- **First Act:** Released dying flora into beautiful crystallization
- **Domain:** Peaceful endings, acceptance, dissolution
- **Following:** Wanderers, mourners, those seeking release

---

### **What Gods Are:**

**Not Human Anymore:**
- Mortal consciousness dissolved
- Divine entity wearing human memories
- Human morality doesn't apply
- Think/perceive on planetary scale
- Motivated by principle compulsion, not human needs

**Capabilities:**
- Manipulate planetary veins at continental scale
- No biological needs (don't eat, sleep, age)
- Perceive reality as overlapping frequencies
- Reshape matter according to principle
- Effectively immortal
- Cannot be killed by conventional means

**Limitations:**
- Bound by principle (cannot act against it)
- Don't communicate with mortals easily (language insufficient)
- Each controls territory but not whole world
- Can conflict with each other
- Jhace's Confluence makes him potential threat

---

## PART 5: COMPLETE COST DOCUMENTATION

### **Vein-Burn (Wholeness):**
- Copper-gold discoloration spreading
- Warm to touch
- Slight pain when using Soulpulse
- Unknown if terminal
- Jhace's burn: ~4.0 cm by N05 end

### **Calcification (Form):**
- Joints hardening progressively
- Reduced flexibility
- Blue-silver discoloration
- Pain during movement
- Tiffani's hands: severe by death (Ch13)

### **Isolation (Purity):**
- Emotional numbness
- Tissue swelling
- Physical sensitivity
- Inability to connect
- Mobel: transformed before terminal progression

### **Vitality Drain (Entropy):**
- Aging effect visible
- Constant fatigue
- Physical weakness
- Existential exhaustion
- Venn: transformed before death

### **Confluence Cost (Jhace Unique):**
- Multiplies all costs simultaneously
- Full Confluence nearly killed him
- Permanent exhaustion afterward
- All four cost types affecting him now
- Uncertain long-term effects

---

## PART 6: POST-TRANSFORMATION WORLD

### **Physical Changes:**

**Vein-Shatter Era Ended:**
- Chronic earthquakes stopped
- Planetary veins stabilized
- New equilibrium reached
- Part of crust broke free during Steal Breaks Open

**Landscape Altered:**
- Some regions levitated/blasted skyward
- Cities devastated anew
- God-domains forming (territories reshaping according to principles)
- Lattice dust composition changed

**Infrastructure:**
- Heat-grid now god-maintained in their territories
- Human maintenance less necessary (but still possible)
- Factional territories now god-claimed
- Independents squeezed out

---

### **Social Changes:**

**Four God-Factions:**
- Xilcore's followers (law, order, geometric perfection)
- Leesa's followers (compassion, healing, mercy)
- Blemo's followers (purity, judgment, zealotry)
- Seeri's followers (acceptance, peaceful endings)

**Human Resistance:**
- Led by Jhace (only human capable of opposing gods)
- Refuses divine authority
- Helps people on own terms
- Small but determined
- Carries Tiffani's memory

**Old Governance:**
- Traditional authorities collapsed
- Guilds/councils defunct
- SoulPulse practitioners split loyalty (gods vs. humans)
- New era beginning

---

## PART 7: TIFFANI'S LEGACY

### **Her Death (N05 Ch12-13):**

**How She Died:**
- Shielded Jhace from falling debris
- Formed final barrier of Form energy
- Debris mortally wounded her
- Died in his arms
- Final words: "I love you" (first and only time)

**Her Sacrifice:**
- Deliberate, split-second choice
- Act of love
- Saved Jhace's life
- Catalyst for his Confluence manifestation
- Indirectly caused god-vessel awakenings

**Her Legacy:**
- Teachings live on through Jhace
- Dual-principle technique now known possible
- Proof that principles can harmonize
- Internal moral compass for Jhace
- Memory drives his resistance

---

## PART 8: COMPLETE SENSORY VOCABULARY

### **Form (Structural):**
- Visual: Blue-silver, geometric, angular, crystalline
- Audio: High chime, crystal ringing, sharp tones
- Tactile: Cool, precise, sharp edges
- Aftermath: Joint stiffness, coldness, mental exhaustion

### **Wholeness (Continuity):**
- Visual: Copper-gold, flowing, organic, branching
- Audio: Mid-range hum, harmonic, musical
- Tactile: Warm, flowing, connecting
- Aftermath: Deep exhaustion, vein-burn growth, identity bleed

### **Purity (Sanctification):**
- Visual: White-gold, blinding, uniform, sterile
- Audio: Piercing tone, single note, painful
- Tactile: Burning, separating, painful
- Aftermath: Tissue swelling, numbness, sensitivity

### **Entropy (Dissolution):**
- Visual: Ash-gray, fading, dispersing, gentle
- Audio: Low hum, soft, fading
- Tactile: Cool release, peaceful, gentle
- Aftermath: Vitality drain, fatigue, aging

### **Confluence (All Four):**
- Visual: All four glows simultaneously, reality warping
- Audio: All four frequencies in impossible harmony
- Tactile: Everything at once, overwhelming
- Aftermath: Nearly fatal, all costs multiplied

---

## PART 9: FACTIONAL SLANG (Updated)

### **God-Factions (New):**
- **Formists:** Xilcore's followers (law, order)
- **Mercybound:** Leesa's followers (compassion)

- **Free Practitioners:** Refuse divine authority

- **Four Principles:** Complete framework
- **Confluence:** All four simultaneously
- **Hollowing:** Terminal condition
- **Vein Network:** Planetary energy channels

# SOULPULSE MAGIC SYSTEM REFERENCE — N04 SCOPE
## "Shatter From Heat" — Limits Discovered, Dual-Principle Revealed

---

## KNOWLEDGE BOUNDARY

**What characters know by end of N04:**
- **Hollowing identified** as terminal condition
- **Dual-principle mastery possible** (Tiffani reveals Form + Wholeness)
- Four principles beginning to be theorized (not yet formalized)
- Strict limits on safe resonance use established
- Infrastructure ~90% restored
- God-vessels approaching transformation (Corlexi Hollows)

**What characters DO NOT know yet:**
- "Four Principles" as complete formal framework
- Confluence (all four principles simultaneously)
- Suppression technology
- God-vessel transformations imminent
- Systematic vein network theory complete

---

## PART 1: HOLLOWING (Terminal Condition Identified)

### **What It Is:**

**Definition:**
Terminal condition where Soulpulse user's conviction fails catastrophically. Irreversible loss of resonance ability. Death of practitioner's connection to Soulpulse.

**Symptoms:**
- Tremors (severe, constant)
- Vein-deadening (ability fades, then vanishes)
- Vacant eyes (thousand-yard stare)
- Inability to spark resonance
- Neurological collapse
- Catatonic state (severe cases)

**Causes:**
- Exceeding safe capacity repeatedly
- Pushing past warning signs
- Conviction failure under extreme stress
- Combination of physical/psychological overload

**Progression:**
1. Warning signs (tremors, difficulty focusing)
2. Reduced capacity (resonance weakens)
3. Intermittent failure (ability comes and goes)
4. Total loss (permanent inability)
5. Catatonia (severe cases)

**Is It Reversible?**
No known cure. Once Hollowed, practitioner never regains ability. Some recover from catatonia, but resonance gone forever.

**Prevention:**
- Respect personal limits
- Don't push past warning signs
- Rest between major uses
- Accept that some things can't be done

---

### **Jhace's Near-Hollowing (N04 Ch2-3)**

**What Happened:**
- Overextended stabilizing geothermal conduit
- Pushed beyond safe capacity
- Severe neurological collapse
- Body shut down, wracked by tremors
- Internal vein-ruptures
- Vision blurred, hands shaking
- Refused to stop until forced
- Collapsed unconscious

**Symptoms:**
- All early Hollowing signs present
- Teetering on edge of terminal condition
- Would have Hollowed if continued
- Saved by Tiffani's intervention

**Recovery:**
- Tiffani used dual-principle healing
- Stabilized vein structure (Form) + healed ruptures (Wholeness)
- Impossible feat thought only Jhace capable of (instinctively)
- Jhace survived but learned harsh lesson

**Lesson Learned:**
- Ambition without caution kills
- Limits exist for reason
- Even "saving people" isn't worth Hollowing
- Sustainable practice only way forward

---

### **Corlexi's Hollowing (N04 Ch8-9)**

**Context:**
- Master architect, god-vessel in early awakening
- Attempted massive showcase construction
- Pushed apprentices beyond limits (two Hollowed mid-ritual)
- Attempted to salvage alone
- Even god-vessel's mortal body has limits

**His Hollowing:**
- Screamed as veins glowed then darkened
- Dropped to knees mid-feat
- Eyes vacant, body shaking
- Fell into catatonic state
- Giant shard crashed aside (couldn't hold)

**Aftermath:**
- Taken by healers
- Fate uncertain
- Myth of invincibility shattered
- Symbol of overreach's cost

**Significance:**
- Even most powerful practitioners can Hollow
- Ambition without limits leads to destruction
- Corlexi's failure taught whole city
- Hollowing epidemic halted by his example

---

## PART 2: DUAL-PRINCIPLE MASTERY (Tiffani's Revelation)

### **What Was Believed Before:**

**Single-Affinity Assumption:**
- Most practitioners have one resonance affinity
- Chloen's multi-affinity seen as rare anomaly
- Only Jhace thought capable of multiple principles (instinctively, during crisis)
- Deliberate multi-principle use thought impossible

**Why Dual-Principle Seemed Impossible:**
- Different frequencies clash (resonance friction)
- Mental focus can't split between contradictory approaches
- Physical cost of one affinity already severe
- Combining two would cause catastrophic failure

---

### **Tiffani's Demonstration (N04 Ch3)**

**Context:**
- Jhace dying from near-Hollowing
- No single-principle approach could save him
- Tiffani revealed hidden capability
- First public dual-principle use

**What She Did:**
- Channeled Form (Structural) to stabilize vein structure
- Simultaneously channeled Wholeness (Continuity) to heal ruptures
- Held both frequencies in perfect balance
- Saved Jhace's life

**How It Looked:**
- Blue-silver (Form) and copper-gold (Wholeness) glows simultaneously
- Geometric patterns overlaying organic healing
- Cool precision + warm flow at once
- Impossible combination working perfectly

**Reaction:**
- Witnesses shocked, awed
- Thought impossible just demonstrated
- Questions raised: Who else can do this?
- Implications: Multi-principle mastery trainable?

---

### **Tiffani's Partial Confession (N04 Ch5)**

**What She Revealed:**
- Trained by exceptional mentor before Piercing
- Learned dual-principle technique deliberately
- Cannot/will not fully explain
- Hints at hidden order or pre-Piercing knowledge

**What She Concealed:**
- Full extent of training
- Who her mentor was (Marisse connection suspected)
- Whether others have this knowledge
- Larger context of her abilities

**Jhace's Response:**
- Chooses trust despite mystery
- Accepts she has reasons for secrecy
- Loves her regardless of unanswered questions
- Relationship deepens through acceptance

**Physical Cost:**
- Dual-principle use accelerates vein-burn growth
- After saving Jhace: Tiffani's burn ~4.2 cm
- Slight tremor, pallor, exhaustion
- Calcification also worsened
- Strain visible but tolerable

---

## PART 3: FOUR PRINCIPLES (Beginning to Theorize)

### **Why Fourth Principle Now Recognized:**

**Observations:**
- Three factions established (Structural, Continuity, Purity)
- Releasers distinct but unclear relationship
- Tiffani's dual-principle demonstration
- Chloen's multi-affinity (deceased but remembered)
- Corlexi's god-vessel stirrings

**Theory Emerging:**
- Not three affinities—four fundamental principles
- Each principle represents aspect of reality
- Practitioners align with principle matching worldview
- Multi-principle mastery possible but rare

**Four Principles (Tentative Framework):**

1. **Form (Structural)**
   - Geometric order, precision, rigidity
   - Inorganic materials
   - Blue-silver, crystalline
   - Cost: Calcification

2. **Wholeness (Continuity)**
   - Connection, healing, flow
   - Organic materials and bonds
   - Copper-gold, warm
   - Cost: Vein-burn, identity bleed

3. **Purity (Sanctification)**
   - Separation, cleansing, judgment
   - Purification and burning
   - White-gold, piercing
   - Cost: Isolation, tissue swelling

4. **Entropy (Dissolution)**
   - Endings, decay, acceptance
   - Controlled release
   - Ash-gray, fading
   - Cost: Vitality drain, aging

**Not Yet Formalized:**
- No unified theory
- No systematic training framework
- No complete understanding of relationships
- Just beginning to see pattern

---

## PART 4: SAFE LIMITS ESTABLISHED

### **Post-Hollowing Guidelines:**

**Personal Limits:**
- Each practitioner has maximum safe capacity
- Varies by individual, affinity, training
- Warning signs must be respected
- Rest periods mandatory

**Warning Signs:**
- Tremors
- Difficulty focusing
- Unusual exhaustion
- Pain during use
- Resonance feeling forced
- Vision changes
- Neurological symptoms

**Recommended Practices:**
- Work within 70% of perceived maximum
- Rest after major uses
- Don't chain multiple large efforts
- Accept that some things can't be done
- Better to fail task than Hollow

**Institutional Changes (Post-Corlexi):**
- Prism imposes strict guidelines
- Guild councils establish standards
- Apprentices taught caution
- Hollowing epidemic halted

---

## PART 5: PHYSICAL COSTS (N04 Progression)

### **Vein-Burn (Continuity):**
- Jhace's burn: ~3.5 cm by N04 end
- Accelerated by near-Hollowing crisis
- Permanent tremor in left hand worsened
- Learns minor self-healing (reduces tremor slightly)

### **Calcification (Structural):**
- Tiffani's hands: noticeable reduction in range
- Dual-principle use worsened condition
- Blue-silver discoloration visible
- Pain during fine work constant
- Uses Soulpulse sparingly now

### **Isolation (Purity):**
- Mobel: extreme isolation, cannot tolerate touch
- Tissue swelling severe
- Emotional numbness total
- Approaching god-vessel transformation (unknowingly)

### **Vitality Drain (Entropy):**
- Venn: appears 10-15 years older than age
- Constant fatigue
- Physical weakness pronounced
- Philosophical acceptance complete
- Approaching god-vessel transformation (unknowingly)

---

## PART 6: INFRASTRUCTURE STATUS

### **Heat-Grid: ~90% Restored**

**What This Means:**
- No longer at risk of imminent collapse
- Daily maintenance manageable
- Natural disaster era ending
- Focus shifts to political conflicts

**Remaining Issues:**
- Some districts still struggling
- Factional territories unequal access
- Maintenance weaponized politically
- Lattice dust corrosion constant

---

## PART 7: GOD-VESSELS APPROACHING (N04 Observations)

### **Four Individuals:**

**Corlexi (Form):**
- Hollowed during showcase
- Catatonic, fate uncertain
- God-compulsion drove him to destruction
- Transformation approaching?

**Mobel (Purity):**
- Extreme isolation
- Physical body failing
- Religious zealotry intensifying
- Something stirring beyond human

**Salee (Wholeness):**
- Network connections deepening
- Sensing districts as extensions of self
- Invisible web of wholeness
- Approaching limits of mortal capacity

**Eries (Entropy):**
- Philosophy spreading rapidly
- Comfort with endings intensifying
- Garden responds to her presence
- Peaceful dissolution emanating

**Characters Don't Know:**
- These four will transform into gods
- Transformation imminent (months away)
- Connection between them
- Their future significance

---

## PART 8: FORBIDDEN KNOWLEDGE (N04 Scope)

**Do NOT reference in N04 prose:**
- "Confluence" (all four principles simultaneously)

**Instead use:**

- Observations without complete understanding

---

**By End of N04, Characters DO NOT Know:**

- Suppression technology exists

- Jhace will manifest Confluence through grief
- Complete vein network theory

# SOULPULSE MAGIC SYSTEM REFERENCE — N03 SCOPE
## "Alloy Folded Wrong" — Weaponization & Political Crisis

---

## KNOWLEDGE BOUNDARY

**What characters know by end of N03:**
- Three factions fully formed (Structuralists, Continuists, Releasers)
- Resonance weaponization (combat applications)
- Lattice dust as environmental hazard
- Shadow grid networks (underground cooperation)
- Fourth principle beginning to emerge (Releasers/Entropy)
- Violence escalating factional divisions

**What characters DO NOT know yet:**
- "Four Principles" as formal framework
- Hollowing as named/terminal condition
- Dual-principle mastery (Tiffani's secret)
- Confluence theory
- Suppression technology
- God-vessel transformations

---

## PART 1: THREE FACTIONS (Fully Crystallized)

### **Structuralists ("The Rigid")**

**Leadership:** Kylar (forge-guild origin, Structural Resonator)
**Philosophy:** Order through regulation; power must be organized; licensing required
**Territory:** Industrial districts, forge-quarters, heat-grid control stations
**Methods:** Bureaucracy, licensing enforcement, territorial exclusion
**Visual Identity:** Blue-silver sashes, geometric insignia
**Membership:** ~35% of practitioners (largest faction)

**Resonance Doctrine:**
- Only licensed practitioners permitted
- Structural work requires certification
- Unlicensed use is illegal in their territory
- Safety through control

**Combat Capabilities:**
- Collapse structures remotely
- Create instant barriers
- Lock opponents in geometric prisons
- Shatter weapons/materials
- Territorial advantage (control infrastructure)

---

### **Continuists ("The Bleeders")**

**Leadership:** Decentralized council; Jhace/Tiffani seen as symbolic figures (unwillingly)
**Philosophy:** Collaboration over control; open access to knowledge; healing-focused
**Territory:** Medical districts, residential areas, refugee settlements
**Methods:** Community organizing, mutual aid, consensus decision-making
**Visual Identity:** Copper-gold armbands (optional, not enforced)
**Membership:** ~40% of practitioners (largest but least organized)

**Resonance Doctrine:**
- Open practice (no licensing)
- Knowledge shared freely
- Anyone may attempt Soulpulse regardless of training
- Healing prioritized over control

**Combat Capabilities:**
- Heal allies mid-battle
- Disrupt enemy connections (painful)
- Sever bonds to disable opponents
- Maintain infrastructure during conflict
- Endurance/self-healing advantage

---

### **Releasers ("The Enders")**

**Leadership:** Venn (glass-guild origin, Dissolution Resonator)
**Philosophy:** Everything ends; we make endings gentle; acceptance over resistance
**Territory:** Burial grounds, waste processing, quarantine zones
**Methods:** Strategic withdrawal, controlled decay, pain management
**Visual Identity:** Ash-gray veils (worn during work)
**Membership:** ~15% of practitioners (smallest but strategically essential)

**Resonance Doctrine:**
- Quiet work (discreet use)
- Endings happen privately
- No loud demonstrations
- Acceptance of inevitable decay

**Combat Capabilities (Emerging Recognition):**
- Accelerate decay in structures/materials
- Peaceful death (mercy killing)
- Controlled dissolution of threats
- Strategic retreat advantage
- Essential services = leverage

**Fourth Principle Recognition:**
- Releasers practice what will become "Entropy principle"
- Not yet formally recognized as fourth principle
- Seen as extension of Purity by some, distinct by others
- Philosophical differences from other three affinities clear

---

## PART 2: RESONANCE WEAPONIZATION

### **Structural Warfare**

**Offensive Techniques:**
- **Collapse Strike:** Remotely destabilize building/structure
- **Barrier Generation:** Instant geometric walls
- **Material Shattering:** Break weapons, tools, armor
- **Geometric Lock:** Trap opponents in crystalline prison
- **Frequency Blade:** Sharpen edge to molecular precision

**Defensive Techniques:**
- **Reinforcement:** Strengthen structures instantly
- **Barrier Walls:** Block attacks with geometric shields
- **Resonance Nullification:** Disrupt enemy Soulpulse
- **Structural Sense:** Detect weaknesses in environment

**Cost in Combat:**
- Rapid calcification during sustained use
- Mental exhaustion from maintaining precision
- Tremors from combat stress
- Joint pain intensifies

---

### **Continuity Warfare**

**Offensive Techniques:**
- **Bond Severing:** Disconnect components (painful, disabling)
- **Vein Disruption:** Interfere with opponent's Soulpulse
- **Connection Overload:** Force sympathetic overload on enemy
- **Network Collapse:** Fail multiple connections simultaneously
- **Identity Bleed Attack:** Force empathic overload (psychological)

**Defensive Techniques:**
- **Rapid Healing:** Mend wounds mid-combat
- **Network Stabilization:** Maintain allies' connections
- **Endurance Boost:** Sustain through continuous use
- **Self-Repair:** Heal self (limited, exhausting)

**Cost in Combat:**
- Vein-burn growth accelerates
- Identity bleed risk increases
- Sympathetic overload more likely
- Exhaustion cumulative, severe

---

### **Purity Warfare**

**Offensive Techniques:**
- **Purging Flame:** Burn "impurities" (including people)
- **Sterile Zone:** Create hostile environment (burns organics)
- **Separation Blast:** Disintegrate materials at molecular level
- **Isolation Field:** Force opponents apart (breaks formations)
- **Cleansing Wave:** Mass purge attack (indiscriminate)

**Defensive Techniques:**
- **Purity Shield:** Block "contaminated" attacks
- **Self-Purification:** Remove toxins, poisons instantly
- **Isolation Bubble:** Protect self through separation
- **Sanctification:** Make area inhospitable to enemies

**Cost in Combat:**
- Tissue swelling worsens rapidly
- Emotional numbness intensifies
- Pain during use extreme
- Isolation tendency becomes pathological

---

### **Releaser Warfare (Emerging)**

**Offensive Techniques:**
- **Decay Acceleration:** Rot structures, materials, flesh
- **Peaceful Release:** Mercy kill (painless, quiet)
- **Controlled Dissolution:** Targeted disintegration
- **Entropy Wave:** Area decay effect (slow but unstoppable)
- **Acceptance Aura:** Psychological attack (induces surrender)

**Defensive Techniques:**
- **Strategic Retreat:** Dissolve obstacles while fleeing
- **Pain Management:** Reduce suffering (self and allies)
- **Controlled Decay:** Safely collapse structures behind them
- **Acceptance:** Endure without fighting (philosophical strength)

**Cost in Combat:**
- Vitality drain (aging effect)
- Fatalism intensifies
- Physical weakness accumulates
- Existential exhaustion

---

## PART 3: LATTICE DUST (Environmental Hazard)

### **What It Is:**

**Composition:**
- Crystallized Soulpulse residue
- Permanent aftermath of Piercing
- Settles everywhere, especially near vein damage
- Mildly corrosive to materials
- Responds to active Soulpulse use

**Effects:**
- **Passive:** Slow corrosion of metal, stone, organic matter
- **Active:** Glows when Soulpulse used nearby
- **Weaponized:** Can be ignited/detonated by Purity users
- **Tracking:** Shows where Soulpulse has been used recently

**Mitigation:**
- Regular cleaning required
- Some areas more saturated than others
- No permanent removal method known
- Becomes environmental fact of life

**Factional Use:**
- Structuralists: Study it, try to contain it
- Continuists: Adapt to it, work around it
- Releasers: Accept it as sign of decay

---

## PART 4: SHADOW GRID NETWORKS

### **What They Are:**

**Definition:**
Underground system of cross-factional cooperation. Workers from all three factions (and independents) collaborate secretly on critical infrastructure, medical care, food distribution. Illegal in Structuralist territory; tolerated elsewhere.

**Operation:**
- Nighttime repairs without permission
- Cross-border medical aid
- Shared knowledge networks
- Mutual aid despite factional divisions

**Jhace/Tiffani's Role:**
- Central coordinators (unwillingly symbolic)
- Connect practitioners across factions
- Prioritize work over politics
- Refuse formal leadership but effectively lead

**Risks:**
- Arrest in Structuralist territory
- Faction retaliation
- Targeted violence (Chloen's death)
- Constant danger

---

## PART 5: CONVERGENCE POINTS

### **Definition:**
Physical locations where factional borders meet. Heavily monitored, tense, but necessary for trade/communication. Jhace/Tiffani use these for network coordination.

**Characteristics:**
- Neutral ground (theoretically)
- All factions patrol
- Violence common
- Essential for cross-border work

**Typical Features:**
- Checkpoint architecture
- Multiple faction guards
- Tense atmosphere
- Quick exits necessary

---

## PART 6: UPDATED PHYSICAL COSTS (N03 Progression)

### **Vein-Burn (Continuity):**
- Jhace's burn: ~3.0 cm by N03 end
- Spreading slowly but steadily
- Warm to touch, slight pain
- Unknown endpoint
- Chloen had multiple small burns (died before progression)

### **Calcification (Structural):**
- Tiffani's hands: noticeable stiffness, reduced range
- Blue-silver discoloration visible
- Pain during fine work
- Progression concerning but not disabling yet

### **Isolation (Purity):**
- Mobel: severely isolated, difficulty with human contact
- Tissue swelling in hands, joints
- Emotional numbness pronounced
- Physical sensitivity extreme

### **Vitality Drain (Releaser/Entropy):**
- Venn: appears older than chronological age
- Fatigue constant
- Philosophical acceptance growing
- Physical weakness accumulating

---

## PART 7: CHLOEN'S MULTI-AFFINITY (Unexplained)

### **Observations:**

**What She Could Do:**
- Heal (Continuity)
- Shape (Structural)
- Possibly others (undeveloped)

**Why Unusual:**
- Most practitioners have single affinity
- Multi-affinity exhausts faster
- Versatility vs. specialization trade-off
- No explanation for why she could

**Her Death:**
- Killed in warehouse massacre (Ch6)
- Didn't get to develop fully
- Mystery of multi-affinity remains
- Jhace suspects others might develop it (including himself, unknowingly)

---

## PART 8: FORBIDDEN KNOWLEDGE (N03 Scope)

**Do NOT reference in N03 prose:**
- "Four Principles" as formal framework (three factions + Releasers observed, but not theorized as four-principle system)
- "Hollowing" as named terminal condition
- Tiffani's dual-principle mastery (secret)
- Confluence theory
- Suppression technology
- God-vessel transformations
- Systematic vein network theory

**Instead use:**
- "Three factions" and "Releasers" (fourth group, distinct philosophy)
- "Resonance burnout" or "sympathetic overload" for what becomes Hollowing
- "Unusual versatility" for Chloen's multi-affinity
- Factional terminology and slang
- Personal observations, political language

---

## PART 9: FACTIONAL SLANG & TERMINOLOGY

### **Structuralist Terms:**

**"The Rigid":** Self-identifier (pride in discipline)
**"Licensed":** Approved practitioner
**"Unlicensed":** Illegal practitioner (derogatory)
**"Geometric Truth":** Structural perfection ideal
**"Frequency Precision":** Technical excellence

### **Continuist Terms:**

**"The Bleeders":** Self-identifier (accepting cost)
**"Open Practice":** Anyone can try
**"Connection Work":** Healing/bonding
**"Network":** Community of mutual aid
**"Bleeding Out":** Sympathetic overload risk

### **Releaser Terms:**

**"The Enders":** Self-identifier (accepting inevitable)
**"Quiet Work":** Discreet practice
**"Peaceful Release":** Mercy/acceptance
**"Everything Ends":** Core philosophy
**"Letting Go":** Acceptance practice

### **Cross-Factional Terms:**

**"Neutrals":** Independents (derogatory from all factions)
**"Shadow Grid":** Underground cooperation network
**"Convergence Points":** Factional borders
**"Lattice Dust":** Environmental hazard
**"Resonance Friction":** Dissonance, conflict

---

## PART 10: N03 CLOSING STATE

**By End of N03, Characters Know:**
- Three factions fully formed, fourth emerging (Releasers)
- Resonance weaponization advanced

- Violence escalating, war looming

**By End of N03, Characters DO NOT Know:**

# SOULPULSE MAGIC SYSTEM REFERENCE — N02 SCOPE
## "Light Cracks Through" — Early Systematization

---

## KNOWLEDGE BOUNDARY

**What characters know by end of N02:**
- Three distinct "resonance affinities" emerging
- Basic resonance mechanics (frequency matching)
- Catastrophic failure modes (vein-snap, cascade, sympathetic overload)
- Physical costs beginning to make sense
- Guild fracture based on affinity differences
- Early factional philosophy forming

**What characters DO NOT know yet:**
- Fourth Principle (Entropy/Dissolution) not formally recognized
- Hollowing as terminal condition (suspected but not confirmed)
- Dual-principle mastery (Tiffani's secret)
- Confluence theory
- Suppression technology
- God-vessel transformations

---

## PART 1: THREE RESONANCE AFFINITIES

### **Structural Affinity (Form)**

**Practitioners:** Tiffani, forge-guild members, architects
**Observable Characteristics:**
- High-pitched crystalline frequency
- Works on inorganic materials (metal, glass, stone)
- Geometric precision
- Cool, sharp sensations
- Blue-silver glow (when visible)

**What They Can Do:**
- Shape materials with precision
- Stabilize structures
- Repair marry points perfectly
- Create intricate joints
- Lock forms in place

**Physical Cost:**
- Joint stiffness (hands especially)
- Calcification (joints slowly hardening over time)
- Mental exhaustion from precision work
- Coldness in extremities
- Tremors from overuse

**Personality Correlation (Observed):**
- Tends toward precision, order
- Values rules and structure
- Perfectionist tendencies
- Intolerant of imprecision

---

### **Continuity Affinity (Wholeness)**

**Practitioners:** Jhace, medical practitioners, repairers
**Observable Characteristics:**
- Mid-range warmth frequency
- Works on organic materials and connections
- Healing and bonding
- Warm, flowing sensations
- Copper-gold glow (when visible)

**What They Can Do:**
- Heal wounds
- Mend connections
- Stabilize failing infrastructure
- Maintain continuity in systems
- Connect disparate elements

**Physical Cost:**
- Vein-burn (mysterious marks growing on skin)
- Exhaustion (deep, bone-tired)
- Temporary tremors
- Identity bleed (feeling others' pain/emotions)
- Warmth depletion afterward

**Personality Correlation (Observed):**
- Tends toward empathy, connection
- Values relationships and community
- Adaptable, flexible
- Difficulty with boundaries

---

### **Purity Affinity (Sanctification)**

**Practitioners:** Mobel, temple keepers, isolationists
**Observable Characteristics:**
- Piercing, clear tone
- Works on separation and purification
- Cleansing but also burning
- Sharp, painful sensations
- White-gold glow (blinding when strong)

**What They Can Do:**
- Cleanse contamination
- Separate impurities
- Purify water/materials
- Create sterile fields
- Burn away corruption

**Physical Cost:**
- Tissue swelling (hands, joints)
- Isolation tendency (emotional numbness)
- Pain during and after use
- Skin sensitivity
- Difficulty connecting with others

**Personality Correlation (Observed):**
- Tends toward absolutism, judgment
- Values purity, separation
- Intolerant of compromise
- Increasing isolation

---

## PART 2: RESONANCE MECHANICS (N02 Understanding)

### **Frequency Matching**

**Basic Principle:**
- Every material has natural frequency
- Practitioner attunes their "pulse" to match
- When frequencies align: sympathetic resonance
- Reality shifts smoothly in response

**How It Works (Observable):**
1. Practitioner focuses on target
2. Senses target's frequency (intuitive)
3. Adjusts internal frequency to match
4. Resonance occurs (tingling, warmth/coolness)
5. Change happens
6. Cost paid (exhaustion, pain, marks)

**Resonance Friction:**
- When frequencies clash instead of matching
- Feels like grinding, resistance
- Causes pain, heat, damage
- Can lead to catastrophic failures

---

### **Catastrophic Failure Modes (N02 Discoveries)**

**Vein-Snap:**
- Material's internal structure breaks under strain
- Sudden, explosive failure
- Can kill bystanders
- Visible as cracks forming instantly
- Caused by excessive force or mismatched frequency

**Resonance Cascade:**
- Failure spreads through connected systems
- One marry point fails → adjacent fail → chain reaction
- Can collapse entire districts
- Visible as wave of failures
- Stopped by breaking connections

**Sympathetic Overload:**
- Practitioner absorbs too much from target
- Identity bleed taken to extreme
- Can lose sense of self
- Jhace experienced this (N02, near-death)
- Leaves lasting damage (tremors, scars)

---

## PART 3: PHYSICAL COSTS (N02 Systematized)

### **Vein-Burn (Continuity Users)**

**What It Is:**
- Mysterious marks appearing on skin
- Copper-gold discoloration
- Grows with repeated use
- Warm to touch
- Slight pain when using Soulpulse

**Progression:**
- Starts small (forearm, hands)
- Spreads slowly over months/years
- Unknown if it stops or kills
- Jhace's burn: ~2.5 cm by N02 end
- Causes: overuse, sympathetic overload

---

### **Calcification (Structural Users)**

**What It Is:**
- Joints slowly hardening
- Reduced flexibility over time
- Hands most affected
- Painful movement
- Blue-silver discoloration (subtle)

**Progression:**
- Starts with stiffness
- Progresses to reduced range of motion
- Unknown if it becomes total
- Tiffani's hands: noticeable stiffness by N02 end
- Causes: high-frequency resonance work

---

### **Isolation Tendency (Purity Users)**

**What It Is:**
- Emotional numbness
- Difficulty connecting with others
- Increasing need for solitude
- Physical sensitivity to touch
- Tissue swelling (hands, joints)

**Progression:**
- Starts with preference for solitude
- Becomes difficulty tolerating company
- Unknown if reversible
- Mobel: increasingly isolated by N02 end
- Causes: separation-based resonance

---

## PART 4: GUILD FRACTURE & FACTIONS

### **Three Emerging Factions (N02)**

**1. Structuralists ("The Rigid")**
- Led by: Forge-guild members, Kylar
- Philosophy: Order through precision, safety through regulation
- Methods: Guild structure, apprenticeships, standards
- Resonance: Structural affinity
- Growing toward: Licensing, control, exclusion

**2. Continuists ("The Bleeders")**
- Led by: Medical practitioners, Jhace's network (informal)
- Philosophy: Connection over control, healing focus
- Methods: Mutual aid, open knowledge-sharing
- Resonance: Continuity affinity
- Growing toward: Community organizing, resistance to regulation

**3. Separatists/Purists (No formal name yet)**
- Led by: Temple keepers, Mobel
- Philosophy: Purity requires separation, magic is sacred
- Methods: Isolation, strict standards, withdrawal
- Resonance: Purity affinity
- Growing toward: Extremism, judgment, exclusion

---

## PART 5: SENSORY DETAILS (N02 Expanded)

### **Structural Resonance (Tiffani's Type)**

**Visual:**
- Blue-silver glow (subtle, geometric patterns)
- Edges sharpen when active
- Crystalline reflections
- Angular light

**Auditory:**
- High-pitched chime
- Crystalline ringing
- Glass-like tones
- Clear, sharp notes

**Tactile:**
- Coolness spreading
- Sharp precision feeling
- Clean, defined edges
- Mental clarity

**Aftermath:**
- Joint stiffness
- Cold extremities
- Mental exhaustion
- Tremors (from precision work)

---

### **Continuity Resonance (Jhace's Type)**

**Visual:**
- Copper-gold glow (warm, flowing)
- Organic patterns (branching, network-like)
- Soft, diffuse light
- Living quality

**Auditory:**
- Mid-range hum
- Harmonic overtones
- Flowing, musical notes
- Warm, resonant tones

**Tactile:**
- Warmth spreading
- Gentle pulling
- Flowing sensation
- Connection feeling

**Aftermath:**
- Deep exhaustion
- Vein-burn growth
- Warmth depletion
- Identity bleed (feeling others)

---

### **Purity Resonance (Mobel's Type)**

**Visual:**
- White-gold glow (blinding when strong)
- Harsh, clear light
- No patterns (uniform)
- Sterile quality

**Auditory:**
- Piercing, clear tone
- Single pure note
- No harmonics
- Sharp, painful sound

**Tactile:**
- Burning sensation
- Separation feeling
- Pain during use
- Clarity but isolation

**Aftermath:**
- Tissue swelling
- Emotional numbness
- Physical sensitivity
- Isolation tendency

---

## PART 6: COMBAT APPLICATIONS (N02 Emerging)

### **Structural Attacks:**
- Collapse structures remotely
- Create barriers instantly
- Lock opponents in place
- Shatter materials
- Defensive: strong barriers

### **Continuity Attacks:**
- Heal allies mid-combat
- Disrupt enemy connections
- Sever bonds (painful)
- Maintain infrastructure during battle
- Defensive: self-healing, endurance

### **Purity Attacks:**
- Burn impurities (including people)
- Create sterile zones (hostile)
- Separate components (disintegration)
- Purge contamination (painful)
- Defensive: isolation fields

- Hollowing as named terminal condition
- Dual-principle mastery (Tiffani's secret)
- Confluence theory
- Suppression devices
- God-vessel transformations
- Systematic vein theory (suspected but not formalized)

**Instead use:**
- "Three resonance affinities" or "three types"
- "Sympathetic overload" for what becomes Hollowing
- Describe Chloen's multi-affinity as unusual, unexplained
- "Resonance friction" for dissonance
- Personal observations and faction-specific terminology

**By End of N02, Characters Know:**
- Three distinct resonance affinities
- Basic frequency-matching mechanics
- Three catastrophic failure modes
- Physical costs systematized
- Guild fracture based on affinity
- Combat applications emerging
- Faction philosophies forming

**By End of N02, Characters DO NOT Know:**
- Fourth principle (Entropy)
- Hollowing as terminal/named condition
- Tiffani's dual-principle ability
- Confluence possibility
- Technical vein network theory
- Suppression technology
- God-vessel potential

**Tone:**
Systematization beginning, fear growing, factions hardening, costs becoming clear, wonder giving way to caution.

# SOULPULSE MAGIC SYSTEM REFERENCE — N01 SCOPE
## "Grip That Holds" — Instinctive Resonance Era

---

## KNOWLEDGE BOUNDARY

**What characters know by end of N01:**
- Magic exists (awakened post-Piercing)
- Instinctive, miraculous, unpredictable
- Manifests differently in different people
- Has physical cost (pain, exhaustion, mysterious burns)
- No systematic understanding yet
- No names for principles or mechanics

**What characters DO NOT know yet:**
- Four Principles framework
- Technical mechanics (frequency, resonance, veins)
- Formal costs or limits
- Hollowing, Confluence, echo stacking
- Faction affiliations based on resonance type

---

## PART 1: BASIC OBSERVATIONS

### **What Is Soulpulse? (N01 Understanding)**

**Observable Phenomena:**
- Magic that responds to will and emotion
- Some people can heal injuries (like Jhace with the child)
- Some people can stabilize structures (Jhace repairing marry points)
- Some people can shape materials (Tiffani with glass)
- Each person's magic feels different

**Common Descriptions:**
- "The world sings along" when it works
- "Warm" vs. "cold" sensations
- Tingling, vibration, pulling feeling
- Material responding as if alive

**Physical Sensations:**
- Warmth spreading through chest/hands
- Tingling in extremities
- Pulling sensation toward target
- Exhaustion afterward
- Sometimes pain (mysterious burns, aches)

---

## PART 2: INSTINCTIVE HEALING (Jhace's Discovery)

### **How Jhace Heals (N01)**

**What It Feels Like:**
- Warmth spreading from chest to hands
- Connection to injured person
- Sensing damage as wrongness
- Guiding healing "like coaxing song"
- Exhaustion afterward

**What He Can Do:**
- Heal wounds (cuts, bruises, broken bones)
- Stop bleeding
- Reduce pain
- Accelerate natural healing
- Works better on simpler injuries

**What He Cannot Do:**
- Raise dead
- Cure diseases instantly
- Heal himself reliably
- Heal multiple people at once (yet)
- Understand how it works

**Physical Cost:**
- Exhaustion (proportional to healing size)
- Mysterious burn on forearm (from scaffolding save, Ch3)
- Tremor in left hand (from overuse)
- Warmth fading afterward (feeling depleted)

---

## PART 3: INSTINCTIVE SHAPING (Tiffani's Ability)

### **How Tiffani Shapes (N01)**

**What It Feels Like:**
- Cool, crystalline clarity
- Sensing structure as geometric patterns
- Guiding material into precise forms
- Mental precision required
- Different exhaustion than Jhace's (sharper, cleaner)

**What She Can Do:**
- Shape glass with unprecedented precision
- Repair marry points perfectly
- Stabilize structures
- Create intricate joints
- Works better on inorganic materials

**What She Cannot Do:**
- Heal living things
- Work on large scales (yet)
- Explain technical basis
- Teach others reliably

**Physical Cost:**
- Mental exhaustion (concentration drain)
- Joint stiffness (hands especially)
- Occasional tremors
- Coolness in extremities

---

## PART 4: OBSERVABLE DIFFERENCES

### **Jhace vs. Tiffani (N01 Observations)**

**Jhace's Magic:**
- Warmth-based
- Works on living things
- Intuitive, emotional
- Exhaustion afterward
- Burn scar from overuse

**Tiffani's Magic:**
- Coolness-based
- Works on structures
- Precision-based, mental
- Joint stiffness afterward
- No visible scars yet

**Speculation (Characters Don't Know):**
- Maybe magic responds to personality?
- Maybe different people have different "types"?
- Maybe training determines ability?
- No systematic understanding yet

---

## PART 5: PHYSICAL COSTS (N01 Knowledge)

### **Known Dangers:**

**Overuse:**
- Severe exhaustion
- Mysterious burns/marks
- Tremors
- Temporary inability to use magic
- Jhace's left hand tremor (permanent)
- Jhace's forearm burn scar (permanent)

**Uncertain Limits:**
- How much is too much? (Unknown)
- Can you die from overuse? (Suspected but unconfirmed)
- Are costs permanent? (Seems so for some)
- Can costs be healed? (Unclear)

**Warning Signs:**
- Extreme exhaustion
- Pain during use
- Trembling
- Coldness or excessive heat
- Difficulty maintaining focus

---

## PART 6: BRAM'S DEATH (N01 Trauma)

### **What Happened:**

**Jhace's Perspective:**
- Attempted to heal Bram (mentor, father-figure)
- Pushed too hard, too long
- Felt something wrong (resistance, wrongness)
- Couldn't save him
- Bram died despite Jhace's efforts

**Lesson Learned:**
- Magic has limits
- Some things can't be healed
- Overuse is dangerous
- Grief doesn't make magic stronger

**Lasting Impact:**
- Jhace more cautious with healing
- Fear of losing people he loves
- Awareness that magic isn't omnipotent
- Burn scar reminder of failure

---

## PART 7: CHLOEN'S DIFFERENCE (N01 Observation)

### **What's Unusual About Chloen:**

**Observable Facts:**
- Can use multiple types of magic
- Heals (like Jhace) AND shapes (like Tiffani)
- Younger, less experienced, but versatile
- Exhausts faster than specialists
- Seems to "bridge" different approaches

**Speculation:**
- Is this normal?
- Is she special?
- Will others develop versatility?
- Unknown

---

## PART 8: FORBIDDEN KNOWLEDGE (N01 Scope)

**Do NOT reference in N01 prose:**
- "Four Principles" or named principles
- "Resonance" as technical term
- "Veins" or "vein network"
- "Hollowing" as condition
- "Confluence" or multi-principle theory
- "Echo stacking"
- "Suppression devices"
- Faction names based on magic type
- God-vessel transformations
- Any systematic theory

**Instead use:**
- "Magic" or "the gift"
- "His ability" or "her power"
- "Different kinds of magic"
- Descriptive sensations (warmth, coolness, tingling)
- Personal observations
- Uncertainty and wonder

---

## PART 9: SENSORY VOCABULARY (N01 Appropriate)

### **Safe Descriptive Language:**

**Jhace's Magic (Warmth-Type):**
- Warmth spreading
- Golden glow (subtle, if visible)
- Tingling sensation
- Gentle pulling
- Exhausting but fulfilling
- Like guiding song

**Tiffani's Magic (Precision-Type):**
- Cool clarity
- Crystalline focus
- Sharp mental precision
- Geometric awareness
- Exhausting but satisfying
- Like solving puzzle

**Physical Sensations:**
- Tingling in extremities
- Warmth or coolness
- Pulling toward target
- Vibration (subtle)
- Exhaustion afterward
- Occasional pain

---

## PART 10: N01 CLOSING STATE

**By End of N01, Characters Know:**
- Magic exists, awakened by Piercing
- Different people have different abilities
- Healing and shaping are distinct
- Magic has physical cost
- Overuse is dangerous
- Some limits exist (can't raise dead)
- Chloen is unusually versatile

**By End of N01, Characters DO NOT Know:**
- Why magic differs between people
- Systematic principles
- Technical mechanics
- Formal limits or theories
- Whether faction-splits will occur
- Anything about god-vessels
- Future developments

**Tone:**
Discovery, wonder, caution, grief. Magic is miraculous but costly, hopeful but dangerous.

---

## END OF N01 SOULPULSE REFERENCE

Use this document for N01 prose generation. Avoid all technical terminology and systematic knowledge not yet discovered in-world.

if os.path.exists(ROOT):
    shutil.rmtree(ROOT)
os.makedirs(ROOT, exist_ok=True)

# --- Helper functions ---
def write(path, content):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(content.strip()+"\n")

def copy_into(src_name, dest_relpath):
    src = f"/mnt/data/{src_name}"
    dst = os.path.join(ROOT, dest_relpath)
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(dst), exist_ok=True)
    if os.path.exists(src):
        shutil.copy2(src, dst)
        return True
    return False
