soulpulse_production = r"""
# Soulpulse Resonance System — Production Canon v1.0

**Purpose:** Lock final, production-ready rules for on-page use of Soulpulse across all books/episodes. This is the baseline for consistency, training new writers, and catching drift.

---

## 0) TL;DR — The Three-Line Rule
1) **It’s resonance, not force.** Effects arise by **attuning** the user’s pulse to the target’s natural frequency.
2) **Costs are mandatory and visible.** **Vein-burn → echo → fatigue/identity tax** track on-page. Hollowing is irreversible.
3) **Four principles, two axes, one paradox:** **Form ↔ Entropy**, **Purity ↔ Wholeness**. **Confluence** = all four at once; terminal for mortals.

---

## 1) Metaphysics
- **World substrate:** A planetary vein-network carries vibrational energy ("Soulpulse"). Every material/life-form has a **natural frequency** (NF).
- **User substrate:** A practitioner’s **soul-frequency** can be modulated via breath, intent, gesture, and tools to match a target’s NF (= **attunement**). 
- **Fields:** Use creates a **pulse-field** (PF) that propagates through local matter and interacts with other PFs (constructive/destructive interference). 
- **Opposition:** Invoking one principle automatically rouses resistance from its opposite. No stable “pure” state exists without a counterforce.

### The Four Principles (operational view)
- **Form (Structure):** impose/restore ideal geometry; reinforce, lock, crystallize; long-lived constructs that still decay over time.
- **Wholeness (Continuity):** knit, link, mend; empathic bridges; stabilize flows; limited cross-material bonding.
- **Purity (Cleansing):** separate, refine, excise; selective burn; judgment-directional and prone to collateral when over-driven.
- **Entropy (Dissolution):** release, end, soften bonds; accelerate decay; nullify constructs and soothe endings.

**Divine opposition pairs:** Form⇄Entropy, Purity⇄Wholeness.

---

## 2) Core Mechanics & Safe Ops

### 2.1 Attunement Protocol (single-user)
**Goal:** establish resonance match with the smallest harmful delta.
1) **Probe:** low-amplitude pulse pings; read tactile/auditory/empathic feedback.
2) **Trim:** micro-adjust breath tempo and focus; bring buzz → hum.
3) **Seat:** hold steady 2–8 breaths to stabilize.
4) **Work:** scale amplitude gradually while monitoring PF stability.
5) **Damp:** active cooldown (grounding, breath reset) to clear **vein-echo**.

*Failure heuristic:* push-through on mismatch = **dissonance → vein-burn → snap**.

### 2.2 Multi-Resonance / “Overtones”
- **Two-tone (dual):** rare, trainable in exceptional users; sharply increases strain. Treat as **hazard class Beta**.
- **Chord (3–4):** unstable; mortals cannot hold safely outside split-second flares.
- **Confluence (all four simultaneous):** **paradox engine.** Mortals: **terminal**. Gods: not achievable (each is a pure aspect). 

### 2.3 Pulse-Field Dynamics
- **Echo Stacking:** residual PF lingers after use; back-to-back workings amplify error. Writers must include either **wait** or **damp** step.
- **Resonance Cascade:** uncontrolled propagation via substrate (structures/veins) causing chain failures, quakes, or collapses.
- **Team Interference:** uncoordinated PFs create feedback. **Stagger** or **choir** (see §2.4) to avoid.

### 2.4 Group Work — Choir & Ring Patterns
- **Duo Harmonic:** lead sets NF; partner rides the overtone. Use for complex repairs or combat shielding.
- **Fivefold Choir (healing):** staggered entries, overlapping 2-breath windows; one **breaker** assigned to cut links on overload.
- **Structural Ring (8–12):** equidistant placement; rotate leads every 3–5 breaths; **anchor** maintains phase clock.

---

## 3) Costs, Injuries, and Failure Modes

### 3.1 Mandatory Costs (choose ≥1 per working on-page)
- **Physio:** tremor, after-heat, joint stiffness (principle-specific manifestations).
- **Psycho:** empathy bleed (Wholeness), perfection fixation (Form), zealotry/isolation (Purity), fatigue/nihilism (Entropy).
- **Systemic:** rising **vein-burn** level; visible channel glow/scar progression.

### 3.2 Progressive Injury Ladder
1) **After-heat / sting** → rest resolves.
2) **Vein-burn** (micro-tears, glow) → requires cooldown & care.
3) **Vein-snap** (channel rupture) → collapse, localized loss of function.
4) **Hollowing** (conviction failure; resonance goes dark) → **irreversible**.

### 3.3 Link-Specific Hazards
- **Sympathetic Overload:** healer shares target’s pain/trauma; requires **breaker**.
- **Identity Bleed:** blurred self/other after repeated Wholeness.
- **Over-Purity:** auto-immolating burn; collateral via over-selection.
- **Over-Form:** calcification/ossification; cognitive rigidity.
- **Over-Entropy:** dissociation, premature aging signatures.

---

## 4) Combat & Field Applications

### 4.1 Techniques (legal for protagonists)
- **Tethering:** latch onto opponent NF to damp/enhance. High-risk; establish cutout.
- **Null Pulse (Entropy):** quick dissolve of enemy constructs or ongoing PFs.
- **Lattice Salves:** prep items that resonate on activation as low-amplitude aids.
- **Pop-up Forts (Form):** short-duration girders/plates; require renewal; expect Purity/Entropy counters.
- **Choir Shields (Wholeness):** rotating duty; explicit strain tracking.

### 4.2 Counters & Anti-magic
- **Suppression Fields:** dissonant blankets that jam PFs; risk of systemic **Cascade** if scaled wide on stressed networks.
- **On-page response:** narrow bandwidth, local dampers, or **go silent** (no PF) until field cycles.

---

## 5) Quantitative Dials (for scene design)
- **Pulse classes:** Micro (tool aid) / Standard (scene beat) / Grand (set-piece). 
- **Breath economy:** Most safe workings resolve in **2–8 breaths**. Anything >12 breaths must show multiple costs.
- **Cooldown:** Minimum **1–3 breaths** quiet after micro; **dozens** after grand; choir requires rotation.
- **Range:** Direct-contact is safest; line-of-sight possible with increased error; long-range via substrates invites Cascade.

---

## 6) Canon-by-Principle (writer crib)

### Form
- **Essence:** order/geometry/reinforcement. 
- **Signatures:** crystalline hum, blue-silver glow, rigidity metaphors.
- **Costs:** stiffness, calcification, rule-obsession. 
- **Antagonisms:** undone by Entropy pulses; brittle under Purity over-selection.

### Wholeness
- **Essence:** mending/linking/stabilizing flows.
- **Signatures:** warm hum, copper-gold light, shared sensation.
- **Costs:** fatigue, identity bleed, sympathetic overload risk.
- **Antagonisms:** severed by Purity; destabilized by heavy Form reconfiguration.

### Purity
- **Essence:** excision/refinement/absolution.
- **Signatures:** white glare, selective burn, narrowing focus.
- **Costs:** inflammation, isolation, zeal escalation; risk auto-immolation at extremes.
- **Antagonisms:** blunted by Wholeness links; rigid Form traps can redirect Purity blasts.

### Entropy
- **Essence:** release/ending/softening bonds.
- **Signatures:** gray hush, wither/flake, easing.
- **Costs:** vitality drain, chill, melancholy, detachment.
- **Antagonisms:** resisted by fresh Form reinforcements; Purity can “burn through” rot if absolutely directed.

---

## 7) Confluence & Endgame Constraints
- **Definition:** full simultaneous resonance of all four principles.
- **Rules:**
  - Mortals: **terminal** (veins calcify/burn out; self-sacrificial window only).
  - Gods: **cannot** Confluence (each is a pure aspect, not a chord).
  - **Stasis constructs** created by Confluence (e.g., fivefold cages) trap; kills require **external teams**.
- **On-page:** display escalating **vein-burn clock**, sensory overload, and macro-environmental hum at distance.

---

## 8) Scene Execution Checklist (drop-in)
**Before:**
- Establish target NF cues (sound/texture/heat/feel). 
- Name principle(s) intended. 
- Define success state and **one** hard limit.

**During:**
- Show probe → trim → seat → work. 
- Log costs (physio/psycho/systemic). 
- Manage echo (pause/damp) or choir rotation.

**After:**
- Show world “ringing” or settling. 
- Update **vein-burn meter** for the user. 
- If group, name the **breaker** status.

---

## 9) Exploit Prevention & Edge Cases
- **No free heals:** Wholeness always trades something (time, pain, fatigue, identity tax).
- **No infinite walls:** Form constructs require renewal; entropy gnaws; Purity and Entropy have clean counters.
- **Purity selectivity cap:** cannot excise beyond user’s discrimination bandwidth; stress widens the cut and raises collateral.
- **Entropy precision:** small, surgical dissolves require calm and practice; panic spreads the rot.
- **Echo discipline:** stacking different principles without damp multiplies dissonance; order your chord deliberately.

---

## 10) Glossary (ops terms)
- **Attunement:** matching one’s pulse to target NF.
- **Pulse-Field (PF):** temporary resonance aura created by use.
- **Vein-echo:** residual vibration in user/environment post-use.
- **Dissonance:** mismatch between pulses → pain/damage/chaos.
- **Vein-burn / Vein-snap:** graded channel injuries (scar vs rupture).
- **Hollowing:** catastrophic conviction failure; permanent.
- **Overtone:** secondary principle layered atop the primary.
- **Breaker:** teammate assigned to sever dangerous links.
- **Choir/Ring:** coordinated group patterns for healing/structure.
- **Tethering:** latching onto another’s NF to modulate it.

---

## 11) Writer Notes & Style
- Use in-world craft verbs: **true, seat, brace, purge, knit, release**. Avoid “cast spell.”
- Track **breaths** and **burn** like stamina bars; make costs legible.
- Echo the **domain aesthetics** in sensory description (geometry/white fire/gold warmth/gray hush).

---

### Change Log
- v1.0 — Initial consolidation for room circulation.
"""
write(os.path.join(docs_root, "01-canon", "soulpulse-resonance-system-production-canon.md"), soulpulse_production)

knowledge_gates = r"""
# N01–N05 Knowledge Gates & Scene Ladder — v1.0

**Purpose:** Hard-stop canon for what characters/world know at each novella (N01–N05), plus drop-in scene templates and lint filters. This prevents anachronistic knowledge, keeps costs visible, and standardizes sensory FX.

## 1) Knowledge Boundary Matrix (Writer-Facing)

| Novella | What Characters Know (Ceiling) | What Characters Do **Not** Know (Redline) |
|---|---|---|
| **N01 — “Grip That Holds”** | Magic is real post-Piercing; instinctive, miraculous, unpredictable. Distinct abilities observed (healing, shaping). Costs exist (pain, exhaustion, burns/tremor). No system. | Any formal terms: **Resonance, Principles, Veins, Hollowing, Confluence, Echo Stacking, Suppression, Factions-by-principle, God-vessels**. |
| **N02 — “Light Cracks Through”** | Three **affinities** emerging (Structural, Continuity, Purity). Frequency matching concept. Failure modes named: **vein-snap, cascade, sympathetic overload**. Costs tracked (vein-burn, calcification, isolation). Faction fracture begins. | No **fourth principle** formalization. No named **Hollowing** (use “burnout/overload”). No dual-principle reveal. No **Confluence**, no suppression tech, no god-vessel concept, no full vein-theory. |
| **N03 — “Alloy Folded Wrong”** | Three factions fully formed; Releasers distinct (fourth **group** emerging). Weaponization of abilities. Lattice dust hazard. Shadow grid networks. Political crisis. | No formal **Four Principles** framework. No named **Hollowing**. No dual-principle. No **Confluence**, suppression tech, god-vessels, or systematic vein theory. |
| **N04 — “Shatter From Heat”** | **Hollowing** identified as **terminal**. **Dual-principle** possible (Tiffani: Form+Wholeness). Four principles **theorized** (not fully formalized). Strict safe-use limits codified. ~90% heat-grid restored. God-vessels **approaching** (unrecognized). | No formal “Four Principles” doctrine. No **Confluence**. No suppression devices. No knowledge of imminent transformations. No complete vein-network theory. |
| **N05 — “Steal Breaks Open”** | **Four Principles formalized. Confluence exists (Jhace only).** Suppression tech exists and fails catastrophically. **Four god-vessel transformations complete** (Xilcore, Leesa, Blemo, Seeri). Vein network understood post-catastrophe. World remade, Era shift. | None of the above should be withheld; this is the **culmination** of discovery for Books 1–5. |

> **Room Rule:** If a draft line violates the Redline column for its novella, flag it `// KNOWLEDGE REDLINE: N0X` during review.

## 2) Health & Cost Clocks (Anchor Values)

**Jhace — Vein-burn (cm, forearm disc):**
- **N01:** present (scaffold incident); unmeasured baseline.
- **N02:** ~2.5 cm; tremor established.
- **N03:** ~3.0 cm; steady spread.
- **N04:** ~3.5 cm; near-Hollowing recovery; partial self-heal learned.
- **N05:** ~4.0 cm; multi-cost stacking begins post-Confluence.

**Tiffani — Calcification (hands):**
- **N01:** stiffness seeds.
- **N02:** noticeable stiffness; pain on fine work.
- **N03:** stiffness + pain sustained; range reduced.
- **N04:** **range notably reduced**; dual-principle worsens; blue-silver discoloration.
- **N05:** **severe** by death; barrier feat pre-Confluence.

**Mobel — Purity Isolation:**
- **N01:** early numbness trend.
- **N02:** isolation + swelling.
- **N03:** severe isolation; sensitivity extreme.
- **N04:** near-transformation affect; body failing.
- **N05:** transforms → **Blemo**.

**Venn/Eries — Entropy Vitality Drain:**
- **N01–N02:** early fatigue.
- **N03:** visibly older; constant fatigue.
- **N04:** weakness + philosophy peak (near-transformation).
- **N05:** transforms → **Seeri**.

> Use these as continuity anchors in beat sheets; deviations require an on-page explanation.

## 3) Sensory FX Ladder (Per Novella)

**Colors, sounds, and tactile cues are permitted only as discovered in-era.**

- **N01:**
  - *Warmth-type (Jhace):* soft golden warmth; gentle hum; connection pull.
  - *Precision-type (Tiffani):* cool crystalline clarity; high chime; sharpened edges.
  - Avoid faction labels; avoid “resonance,” “frequency,” or principle names.

- **N02:**
  - Introduce **frequency matching** language and the three affinity identities.
  - Allow failure-mode terms (**vein-snap, cascade, sympathetic overload**).

- **N03:**
  - Weaponization FX allowed (barriers, prisons, decay auras) with **cost beats**.
  - Lattice dust: glows on use; corrosive residue.

- **N04:**
  - Add **Hollowing** nomenclature and caution rituals; dual-principle visuals (blue-silver + copper-gold overlay).

- **N05:**
  - Full palette active: four glows concurrently during **Confluence**, world-scale PF ripples, suppression-field failure visuals, god-vessel ascensions.

## 4) Scene Header & Ladder Template (Drop-In)

**Header (Te’Oga standard):**
`Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting 431 — Coreven—Underface`
`4/5/7/431 — Coreven—Underface`

**Scene Ladder Fields (fill per scene):**

- **Knowledge Ceiling:** (auto-filled from §1)
- **Principle Usage:** None / Form / Wholeness / Purity / Entropy / Dual / Confluence
- **Breath Budget:** Micro (2–3) / Standard (4–8) / Grand (9–12+)
- **Cost Beats:** Physio / Psycho / Systemic (Vein-burn stage: __ )
- **Failure Safeguards:** Breaker? Choir? Damp window?
- **Forbidden Flags:** (terms/tech restricted by era)
- **Continuity Pins:** Jhace burn size; Tiffani mobility; Mobel isolation; Venn vitality.
- **Aftermath FX:** echo, dust glow, environmental ringdown.

> Paste this block atop every new scene card; the knowledge gate becomes muscle memory.

## 5) Era Lint Pack (Regex & Review Notes)

**N01:**
- Ban: `resonance|principle|veins?|Hollowing|Confluence|suppression|faction(s)?|god-?vessel(s)?`
- Replace **“magic/miracle/gift”** for system terms.

**N02:**
- Allow: `resonance`, `frequency matching`, and failure-mode terms.
- Ban: `four principles|Hollowing|dual-?principle|Confluence|suppression|god-?vessel(s)?`

**N03:**
- Allow faction names; allow weaponization terms.
- Ban: `four principles` (as a formal doctrine), `Hollowing` (as a named medical), `dual-?principle`, `Confluence`, `suppression`, `god-?vessel(s)?`.

**N04:**
- Allow: `Hollowing`, dual-principle visuals.
- Ban: explicit **Confluence**, `suppression`, foreknowledge of god-transformation, complete vein-network theory.

**N05:**
- All terms unlocked; ensure **order-of-revelation** is dramatized on page.

> Use editor search with case-insensitive regex during copyedits.

## 6) Ops Cards (One-Pagers per Novella)

**N01 Ops Card**

# --- Tools: Linters ---
lexicon_lint_py = r"""
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
lexicon_lint_py += r'''
import sys, re, os, argparse

SUBSTITUTIONS = [
    (re.compile(r"\bweeks?\b", re.I), "anneal/anneals"),
    (re.compile(r"\bmonths?\b", re.I), "crucible/crucibles"),
    (re.compile(r"\byears?\b", re.I), "casting/castings"),
    (re.compile(r"\bhours?\b", re.I), "tides/breaths (context)"),
    (re.compile(r"\bminutes?\b", re.I), "breaths/strokes (context)"),
    (re.compile(r"\bradio|broadcast|airwaves\b", re.I), "bell-line/crier/signal board"),
    (re.compile(r"\bphone|call|text\b", re.I), "runner/bellman/notice slate"),
    (re.compile(r"\belectric(ity|al)?|power grid\b", re.I), "heat-grid/pressure-lines"),
    (re.compile(r"\bpolice|cops\b", re.I), "guard cohort/Bureau agents"),
    (re.compile(r"\bhospital|ER\b", re.I), "clinic hall/recovery ward/quench-hall"),
    (re.compile(r"\bGPS|map app\b", re.I), "route slate/surveyor’s marks"),
]

def scan_file(path):
    hits = []
    try:
        with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
            text = f.read()
    except Exception as e:
        return hits
    for rx, repl in SUBSTITUTIONS:
        for m in rx.finditer(text):
            start = max(0, m.start()-40)
            end = min(len(text), m.end()+40)
            ctx = text[start:end].replace("\n"," ")
            hits.append((path, m.group(0), repl, ctx))
    return hits

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Lexicon linter (Te’Oga substitutions)")
    ap.add_argument("paths", nargs="+")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    files = []
    for p in args.paths:
        if os.path.isdir(p):
            for root, _, fs in os.walk(p):
                for fn in fs:
                    if fn.lower().endswith((".md", ".txt", ".markdown")):
                        files.append(os.path.join(root, fn))
        else:
            files.append(p)

    any_hits = False
    for fpath in sorted(files):
        for path, term, repl, ctx in scan_file(fpath):
            any_hits = True
            print(f"[LEXICON] {path}: '{term}' -> suggested '{repl}'")
            print(f"  ...{ctx}...")
    if any_hits:
        print("\nLexicon linter found drift. Please replace terms.")
        sys.exit(1)
    else:
        print("Lexicon linter: clean.")
        sys.exit(0)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
'''
write(os.path.join(ROOT, "tools", "lint", "lexicon_lint.py"), lexicon_lint_py)

knowledge_gate_lint = r"""
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
knowledge_gate_lint += r'''
import sys, os, re, argparse

BANS = {
    "N01": re.compile(r"\b(resonance|principle|veins?|Hollowing|Confluence|suppression|factions?|god-?vessels?)\b", re.I),
    "N02": re.compile(r"\b(four principles|Hollowing|dual-?principle|Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\b", re.I),
    "N03": re.compile(r"\b(four principles|Hollowing|dual-?principle|Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\b", re.I),
    "N04": re.compile(r"\b(Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\b", re.I),
    "N05": None,
}

def scan_file(path, era):
    rx = BANS.get(era)
    if not rx:
        return []
    try:
        txt = open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").read()
    except:
        return []
    hits = []
    for m in rx.finditer(txt):
        start = max(0, m.start()-40)
        end = min(len(txt), m.end()+40)
        ctx = txt[start:end].replace("\n"," ")
        hits.append((m.group(0), ctx))
    return hits

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Knowledge Gate linter")
    ap.add_argument("--era", required=True, choices=["N01","N02","N03","N04","N05"])
    ap.add_argument("paths", nargs="+")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    files = []
    for p in args.paths:
        if os.path.isdir(p):
            for root, _, fs in os.walk(p):
                for fn in fs:
                    if fn.lower().endswith((".md",".markdown",".txt")):
                        files.append(os.path.join(root, fn))
        else:
            files.append(p)

    any_hits = False
    for f in sorted(files):
        hits = scan_file(f, args.era)
        for term, ctx in hits:
            any_hits = True
            print(f"[GATE {args.era}] {f}: term '{term}' not allowed")
            print(f"  ...{ctx}...")
    if any_hits:
        print(f"\nKnowledge Gate {args.era} violations found.")
        sys.exit(1)
    else:
        print(f"Knowledge Gate {args.era}: clean.")
        sys.exit(0)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
'''
write(os.path.join(ROOT, "tools", "lint", "knowledge_gate_lint.py"), knowledge_gate_lint)

# Utility: header generator
header_gen = """#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, argparse

TEMPLATE = "Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting {casting} — {location}\\n{d}/{a}/{c}/{casting} — {location}\\n"

def main():
  ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Generate Te’Oga scene headers")
  ap.add_argument("--casting", required=True, help="Casting year")
  ap.add_argument("--d", required=True, help="Tide number")
  ap.add_argument("--a", required=True, help="Anneal number")
  ap.add_argument("--c", required=True, help="Crucible number")
  ap.add_argument("--location", required=True, help="Location string")
  args = ap.parse_args()
  print(TEMPLATE.format(casting=args.casting, d=args.d, a=args.a, c=args.c, location=args.location))

if __name__ == "__main__":
  main()
"""
write(os.path.join(ROOT, "tools", "templates", "generate_scene_header.py"), header_gen)

def write(path, content):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(content.rstrip()+"\n")

    rollup_block = "\n".join(rollup)

    # Continuity anchors snapshot up to this era
    cont_lines = ["### Continuity Anchors (Rollup)\n"]
    for k, vals in ANCHORS.items():
        # slice values up to index i (guard)
        if i <= len(vals):
            cont_lines.append(f"- **{k}:** " + "; ".join(vals[:i]))
        else:
            cont_lines.append(f"- **{k}:** " + "; ".join(vals))
    cont_block = "\n".join(cont_lines)

    ladder = textwrap.dedent(f"""\

    ## Chapter List (Ch01–Ch15)

    - Ch02 —
    - Ch03 —
    - Ch04 —
    - Ch05 —
    - Ch06 —
    - Ch07 —
    - Ch08 —
    - Ch09 —
    - Ch10 —
    - Ch11 —
    - Ch12 —
    - Ch13 —
    - Ch14 —
    - Ch15 —

    ## Notes
    - If {era} deviates from the anchor values, justify on-page (injury, rest, or new technique).
    - Keep sensory FX era-appropriate; no leakage from later lexicon.
    """)
    write(os.path.join(ERA_DIR, "ladder.md"), ladder)

    # Chapter stubs
    for ch in range(1,16):
        ch_name = f"Ch{ch:02d}.md"
        stub = SCENE_TEMPLATE.format(era=i)
        write(os.path.join(CH_DIR, ch_name), stub)

# Zip updated repo
zip_path = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible.zip"
if os.path.exists(zip_path):
    os.remove(zip_path)
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
    for folder, _, files in os.walk(ROOT):
        for fn in files:
            full = os.path.join(folder, fn)
            z.write(full, os.path.relpath(full, ROOT))

# Scaffold N06–N30 ladders with escalating detail tiers and create ops-decks for N16–N30
import os, textwrap, zipfile, shutil

ROOT = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible"
assert os.path.exists(ROOT), "Base repo not found; run previous step first."
NOV_ROOT = os.path.join(ROOT, "docs", "04-plot", "novellas")

os.makedirs(NOV_ROOT, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(OPS_ROOT, exist_ok=True)

# Tiers mapping
def tier_for(n):
    if 6 <= n <= 10: return "Tier A — Structured Beats"
    if 11 <= n <= 15: return "Tier B — Decision Trees"
    if 16 <= n <= 20: return "Tier C — Ops-Backed Ladders"
    if 21 <= n <= 25: return "Tier D — Timestamped Ladders"
    if 26 <= n <= 30: return "Tier E — Final Ops Decks"
    return "Tier ?"

def chapter_template(n):
    # Return per-chapter template string by tier
    if 6 <= n <= 10:
        return textwrap.dedent(f"""
        # Chapter Ladder — N{n:02d}

        **Tier:** Structured Beats (8–12 bullets)

        **Header (Te’Oga):**
        `Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting ____ — Location`
        `d/a/c/____ — Location`

        ## Knowledge Gate
        - Inherits N01–N05 rollup; all terms permitted **only** if known by POV at this point.
        - Enforce cost visibility on every working.

        ## Beats (8–12)
        - [ ] Beat 1 —
        - [ ] Beat 2 —
        - [ ] Beat 3 —
        - [ ] Beat 4 —
        - [ ] Beat 5 —
        - [ ] Beat 6 —
        - [ ] Beat 7 —
        - [ ] Beat 8 —
        - [ ] (optional) Beat 9 —
        - [ ] (optional) Beat 10 —
        - [ ] (optional) Beat 11 —
        - [ ] (optional) Beat 12 —

        ## Breath Budget
        - Micro (2–3) / Standard (4–8) / Grand (9–12+)

        ## Cost Beats (check ≥1)
        - Physio / Psycho / Systemic (Vein-burn stage: __ )

        ## Continuity Pins
        - Jhace burn | Tiffani mobility | Mobel isolation | Venn vitality.

        ## Aftermath FX
        - Echo / dust glow / ringdown.
        """).strip()+"\n"
    if 11 <= n <= 15:
        return textwrap.dedent(f"""
        # Chapter Ladder — N{n:02d}

        **Tier:** Decision Trees

        **Header (Te’Oga):**
        `Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting ____ — Location`
        `d/a/c/____ — Location`

        ## Knowledge Gate

        - [ ] ...

        - **Primary Choice:** (A) ___ vs (B) ___
        - **Branch Consequences:**

        - [ ] Failure mode 1 → mitigation
        - [ ] Failure mode 2 → mitigation

        ## Choir Usage Notes
        - Roles: Lead / Overtone / Breaker / Anchor
        - Rotation: __ breaths

        - If applicable (1 in 3 chapters): [ ] Insert brief enemy POV here.

        ## Costs & Continuity
        - Breath budget; cost beats; pins updated.
        """).strip()+"\n"
    if 16 <= n <= 20:
        return textwrap.dedent(f"""
        # Chapter Ladder — N{n:02d}

        **Tier:** Ops-Backed Ladders

        **Header (Te’Oga):**
        `Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting ____ — Location`

          - __:__ —

    if 21 <= n <= 25:

        # Chapter Ladder — N{n:02d}

        **Tier:** Timestamped Ladders

        `Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting ____ — Location`
        `d/a/c/____ — Location`

        - __:__ —
        - __:__ —

    if 26 <= n <= 30:

        - Plan C: __

        ## Costs & Continuity
        - Breath budget; cost beats; pins updated.
        """).strip()+"\n"
    return "# TODO\n"

def ladder_doc(n):
    tier = tier_for(n)
    knowledge = textwrap.dedent("""\
    **Knowledge Rollup:** Inherits N01–N05 canon (terms unlocked post-N05). Maintain local secrecy constraints by POV and scene timing. All costs remain mandatory.
    """)
    chapters = "\n".join([f"- Ch{c:02d} —" for c in range(1,16)])
    return textwrap.dedent(f"""
    # Novella Ladder — N{n:02d}

    **Tier:** {tier}

    **Purpose:** Standardized scaffold inheriting prior knowledge and continuity; escalates operational detail appropriate to tier.

    ## Knowledge & Continuity
    {knowledge}

    ## Chapter List (Ch01–Ch15)
    {chapters}

    ## Notes
    - Keep sensory FX consistent with principle aesthetics.
    - Update ledgers in each chapter stub.
    """)

# Create ladders and chapter stubs
for n in range(6, 31):
    ERA = f"N{n:02d}"
    ERA_DIR = os.path.join(NOV_ROOT, ERA)
    os.makedirs(ERA_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    CH_DIR = os.path.join(ERA_DIR, "chapters")
    os.makedirs(CH_DIR, exist_ok=True)

    with open(os.path.join(ERA_DIR, "ladder.md"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(ladder_doc(n))

    template = chapter_template(n)
    for ch in range(1,16):
        with open(os.path.join(CH_DIR, f"Ch{ch:02d}.md"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write(template)

# Update novellas index to include N01–N30
index_path = os.path.join(NOV_ROOT, "INDEX.md")
lines = ["# Novella Ladders Index\n"]
for i in range(1, 31):
    lines.append(f"- [N{i:02d}](./N{i:02d}/ladder.md)")
with open(index_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n".join(lines)+"\n")

# Create Ops Decks for N16–N30
def ops_deck_doc(n):
    return textwrap.dedent(f"""
    # Ops Deck — N{n:02d}

    **Tier:** {tier_for(n)}

    ## Timeline (tide:breaths)
    - __:__ —
    - __:__ —
    - __:__ —

    ## Comms & Roles
    - Lead | Overtone | Breaker | Anchor | Extraction

    ## Strength/Morale/Resources
    | Unit/Team | Start | Losses | End | Notes |
    |---|---:|---:|---:|---|
    | | | | | |

    ## Anti-Magic & Field Effects
    - Suppression counters, silent windows, dampers

    ## Contingencies
    - Plan B / Plan C / Abort criteria
    """)

for n in range(16, 31):
    era_dir = os.path.join(OPS_ROOT, f"N{n:02d}")
    os.makedirs(era_dir, exist_ok=True)
    with open(os.path.join(era_dir, "ops-deck.md"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(ops_deck_doc(n))

# Re-zip repository
zip_path = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible.zip"
if os.path.exists(zip_path):
    os.remove(zip_path)
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
    for folder, _, files in os.walk(ROOT):
        for fn in files:
            full = os.path.join(folder, fn)
            z.write(full, os.path.relpath(full, ROOT))

[USER]
and what will this git repo allow or could be used for?

[ASSISTANT]
In plain terms: this repo turns your sprawling saga into a **single source of truth** with guardrails. It’s built for teams and scale. Here’s what it lets you do—cleanly, repeatedly, without “who changed what?” drama.

## What you can use it for
- **Room coordination (at speed):** Everyone works from the same ladders, ops decks, and canon. Issues/PR templates force disciplined changes and capture canon impact.
- **Canon enforcement in code:** CI runs custom linters that slap hands when someone types “week” instead of **anneal** or leaks **Confluence** into N03. No more vibe-based edits—rules are executable.
- **Continuity at a glance:** Each novella (N01–N30) has its own ladder, chapter stubs, knowledge rollup, and health/cost anchors. You can track Jhace’s burn, Tiffani’s calcification, etc., without spreadsheets going feral.
- **Operational planning:** N16–N30 include ops decks with timelines, comms, strength/morale/resources tables, anti-magic counters, and contingencies. It’s a war room, not a diary.
- **Onboarding ammo:** New writers get canon, magic system, lexicon, and scene templates in one place. Less “where’s that doc?” more “here’s the ladder—fill it.”
- **Versioned decisions:** Pull requests document *why* something changed (“Canon Impact” section), so future-you can audit choices instead of guess.
- **Milestones & burn-down:** Novella folders + chapter stubs make progress trackable (per chapter, per tier). Easy to wire into GitHub Projects for dashboards.
- **Adaptation readiness:** Ops-first structure (timelines/maps/kill-chains) is exactly what producers, game designers, and VFX need when translating beats to screens/systems.

## Day-to-day workflow (how it actually gets used)
1. **Branch:** `git switch -c N09-ch03-draft`
2. **Write:** fill `docs/04-plot/novellas/N09/chapters/Ch03.md` using the scaffold.
3. **Self-check:**  
   - `make lint`  
   - Or run:  
     `python tools/lint/lexicon_lint.py docs/04-plot/novellas/N09/chapters/Ch03.md`  
     `python tools/lint/knowledge_gate_lint.py --era N09 docs/04-plot/novellas/N09/`
4. **PR:** open PR, explain canon impact, CI runs the same checks.
5. **Review & merge:** green checks = ship. Redlines point to exact lines to fix.

## Extras the repo enables (when you’re ready)
- **Docs site** (MkDocs/Docusaurus) that auto-publishes canon and ladders from `/docs`.
- **Pre-commit hooks** so lint runs before any commit reaches GitHub.
- **CSV/board exports** for Strength/Morale ledgers and a “who dies where” matrix.
- **Exporters** (Fountain/FDX/Notion) so writers can draft in their poison but stay in canon.

TL;DR: this isn’t a pretty folder—it’s a **production pipeline**. It keeps language, rules, pacing, and operations consistent while letting a room of humans move fast without breaking myth.

[USER]
now how could an ai model use this?

[ASSISTANT]
Short version: turn the repo into a **brain you can query**, a **rulebook the AI must obey**, and a **bot that polices PRs**. Here’s how.

# 1) Retrieval-Augmented Brain (RAG)
Index `/docs` so the model answers from canon, not vibes.

- **Chunking:** split by headings; keep titles and file paths as metadata.  
- **Indices:**  
  - `canon_index` → `/docs/01-canon/*` (lexicon, magic, gates)  
  - `novella_index` → `/docs/04-plot/novellas/N**/ladder.md`  
  - `chapter_index` → chapter stubs  
  - `ops_index` → `/docs/05-ops/ops-decks/*`
- **Record schema (example):**
```json
{
  "id": "N21/chapters/Ch03",
  "era": "N21",
  "type": "chapter_stub",
  "path": "docs/04-plot/novellas/N21/chapters/Ch03.md",
  "headings": ["Breath Budget","Cost Beats","Continuity Pins"],
  "text": "<content>",
  "tags": ["Wholeness","Entropy","choir","breaker"]
}
```
- **Query pattern:** “Answer using only canon; cite `path`. If a rule is missing, propose as *speculative*.”

# 2) Hard Guardrails (tools the model must call)
Wrap your existing linters and rules as functions. The model generates → calls tools → self-corrects.

**Function contracts:**
```json
get_knowledge_rollup(era)         // returns allowed/forbidden terms
lint_lexicon(text)                // returns drift hits (week→anneal, etc.)
lint_knowledge(text, era)         // returns forbidden-term hits for that era
get_health_anchors(era)           // returns Jhace/Tiffani/Mobel/Eries expected states
get_scene_template(era, tier)     // returns the correct scaffold
```
**Loop:**
1) Draft beats.  
2) `lint_lexicon` + `lint_knowledge`.  
3) If violations → auto-rewrite.  
4) Compare beats against `get_health_anchors` and flag continuity mismatches.  
5) Output *only* when clean; otherwise return “violations + fixed draft”.

# 3) Task Packs the AI can do well
- **Fill a chapter stub:** Pull ladder + gate + anchors → produce 8–14 beats, breath budgets, cost beats, aftermath FX.  
- **Continuity audit:** Ingest a draft; confirm era-safe vocabulary, costs-per-working, and anchor deltas.  
- **Ops expansion (N16–N30):** Turn ops deck into timestamped sequences; compute casualty ceilings and update Strength/Morale tables.  
- **PR cop:** On every pull request, the bot comments: linters, rule citations, suggested Te’Oga substitutions, and a 1-paragraph risk summary.

# 4) Prompt contract (don’t let it freestyle)
System prompt core:
- “You are **Story Bible Enforcer**. You must obey Knowledge Gates and Lexicon. Never invent canon; mark new ideas as **Proposal** with justification. Every magical use must show at least one **cost**. Use Te’Oga time units.”

Add **few-shots**:
- One compliant scene ladder.  
- One rejected draft with violations → corrected version.

# 5) GitHub Integration (zero ceremony)
- **Action step:** Add a workflow that runs:  
  1) `tools/lint/*.py` (already shipped)  
  2) `ai_review.py` (calls the model with RAG, posts PR review comment)
- **Policy:** Block merge on lexicon/knowledge violations, allow merge with AI suggestions on style.

# 6) Fine-tune vs. Inference-time
- **Don’t fine-tune canon.** Keep rules live in RAG so updates hit instantly.  
- **Do fine-tune style** (beat density, ops tone) if you want consistent scaffolding, but keep it narrow.

# 7) Example end-to-end
“Generate N09/Ch03”
1) Pull `N09/ladder.md` + rollup + anchors.  
2) Draft beats (Tier B decision tree).  
3) Run linters; fix violations.  
4) Emit Markdown into `docs/04-plot/novellas/N09/chapters/Ch03.md`.  
5) Open a PR with an **Impact on Canon** section (usually “None”).

# 8) What this prevents
- Era leaks (“Confluence” in N03).  
- Lexicon drift (“week/month/year”).  
- Costless magic.  
- Continuity rot (Jhace’s burn size hopping around).  
- Room confusion about who changed what and why.

If you want this wired in, I can drop an `/ai/` folder with: RAG config, prompt packs, tool wrappers for the linters, and a PR-review GitHub Action that does the whole loop automatically.

[USER]
that would be great

[ASSISTANT]
# Add an /ai folder with RAG config, prompts, tool wrappers, and a PR-review GitHub Action
import os, textwrap, json, zipfile, shutil, re, subprocess, pathlib

ROOT = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible"
assert os.path.exists(ROOT), "Repo missing; generate it first."

AI_ROOT = os.path.join(ROOT, "ai")
os.makedirs(AI_ROOT, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "prompts"), exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "index"), exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "tools"), exist_ok=True)

# README for AI folder
readme_ai = """# AI Assistant

This folder contains a minimal Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) setup and a **PR Review bot** that enforces canon, lexicon, and knowledge gates.

## Components
- `config.yaml` — what to index and how to chunk.
- `prompts/` — system prompt and few-shots.
- `index/build_index.py` — chunks `/docs` and writes `index.jsonl` with metadata.
- `ai_review.py` — orchestrates: builds index, diffs changed files, runs linters, retrieves canon context, and writes a PR comment.
- `tools/ai_stub.py` — optional model call wrapper (uses `OPENAI_API_KEY` if present).

## Usage (local)
```
python ai/index/build_index.py
python ai/ai_review.py --base main --head HEAD
```

## GitHub Action
`.github/workflows/ai-review.yml` runs `ai_review.py` on pull requests and posts a comment with violations + citations.
"""
with open(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "README.md"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(readme_ai)

# config.yaml
config_yaml = """# RAG/Review Config
index_roots:
  - docs/01-canon
  - docs/04-plot/novellas
  - docs/05-ops
chunk:
  max_chars: 1800
  overlap: 200
file_globs:
  - "**/*.md"
  - "**/*.txt"
"""
with open(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "config.yaml"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(config_yaml)

# prompts
system_prompt = """You are **Story Bible Enforcer** for the Confluence Chronicles.
Rules:
- Obey Knowledge Gates per novella (N01–N30).
- Enforce Te’Oga lexicon (tide/anneal/crucible/casting).
- Every magical working must show ≥1 cost (physio/psycho/systemic).
- Never invent canon; mark anything new as *Proposal* and justify.
- Cite sources using repo paths (e.g., docs/01-canon/master-lexicon.md)."""
fewshot_ok = """### Example — Compliant Scene Ladder (N09)
- Era Gate: N09
- Knowledge: Confluence not named; Hollowing not medicalized.
- Beats:
  - Breach team rotates choir shield (Wholeness) for 6 breaths.
  - Jhace seats to Form, creates short-span braces; costs: tremor + after-heat.
  - Failure branch: lattice dust threatens cascade; breaker cuts link.
- Breath Budget: 4–8
- Costs: Physio + Systemic (vein-burn + fatigue)
- Aftermath FX: low hum, dust glow settles."""
fewshot_violation = """### Example — Rejection (Violation) and Fix
**Draft line:** "After an hour, they used Confluence to call the cops."
**Violations:** 'hour' (lexicon), 'Confluence' (N09 leak), 'cops' (lexicon).
**Fix:** "After two dozen breaths, they layered Form and Wholeness—no full chord—and signaled the guard cohort.""""
with open(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "prompts", "system.md"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(system_prompt+"\n\n"+fewshot_ok+"\n\n"+fewshot_violation+"\n")

# Simple indexer
indexer = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, re, argparse, pathlib, yaml, glob, hashlib

def load_config(path):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return yaml.safe_load(f)

def read_text(path):
    try:
        return open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").read()
    except:
        return ""

def chunk_text(text, max_chars=1800, overlap=200):
    chunks = []
    start = 0
    n = len(text)
    while start < n:
        end = min(n, start + max_chars)
        # try not to cut in the middle of a paragraph
        cut = text.rfind("\n\n", start, end)
        if cut == -1 or cut <= start + 200:
            cut = end
        chunks.append(text[start:cut])
        start = max(cut - overlap, cut)
    return [c for c in chunks if c.strip()]

def path_tags(path):
    tags = []
    if "/novellas/" in path:
        m = re.search(r"/novellas/(N\d{2})", path)
        if m: tags.append(m.group(1))
    if "/01-canon/" in path:
        tags.append("canon")
    if "/05-ops/" in path:
        tags.append("ops")
    return tags

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--config", default="ai/config.yaml")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default="ai/index/index.jsonl")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    cfg = load_config(args.config)
    roots = cfg["index_roots"]
    patterns = cfg["file_globs"]
    max_chars = cfg["chunk"]["max_chars"]
    overlap = cfg["chunk"]["overlap"]

    records = []
    for root in roots:
        for pat in patterns:
            for path in glob.glob(os.path.join(root, pat), recursive=True):
                if not os.path.isfile(path): continue
                txt = read_text(path)
                for i, ch in enumerate(chunk_text(txt, max_chars, overlap)):
                    rid = hashlib.md5(f"{path}:{i}".encode()).hexdigest()
                    rec = {
                        "id": rid,
                        "path": path.replace("\\","/"),
                        "chunk_id": i,
                        "text": ch,
                        "tags": path_tags(path),
                    }
                    records.append(rec)

    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(args.out), exist_ok=True)
    with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for r in records:
            f.write(json.dumps(r, ensure_ascii=False)+"\n")
    print(f"Wrote {len(records)} chunks to {args.out}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
"""
with open(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "index", "build_index.py"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(indexer)

# AI stub (optional)
ai_stub = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os

def generate_review(prompt, system=None):
    """ + '"""' + r"""
    Placeholder for LLM call. If OPENAI_API_KEY is present, you can extend this function
    to call your provider. This repo does not include any vendor SDKs by default.
    Returns None by default so the pipeline falls back to rule-based output.
    """ + '"""' + r"""
    api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        return None
    # TODO: implement provider call.
    return None
"""
with open(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "tools", "ai_stub.py"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(ai_stub)

# PR review orchestrator
ai_review = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, subprocess, re, sys, glob, argparse, textwrap

REPO_ROOT = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), ".."))
LEX_LINT = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "tools", "lint", "lexicon_lint.py")
KG_LINT = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "tools", "lint", "knowledge_gate_lint.py")
INDEX_PATH = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "ai", "index", "index.jsonl")

def run(cmd):
    p = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True)
    out,_ = p.communicate()
    return p.returncode, out

def changed_files(base, head):
    # Try to diff; fall back to all docs
    rc, out = run(["git", "diff", "--name-only", f"{base}...{head}"])
    paths = [l.strip() for l in out.splitlines() if l.strip()]
    md = [p for p in paths if p.endswith((".md",".txt"))]
    if not md:
        for root, _, files in os.walk("docs"):
            for fn in files:
                if fn.endswith((".md",".txt")):
                    md.append(os.path.join(root, fn))
    return sorted(set(md))

def infer_era(path):
    m = re.search(r"/novellas/(N\d{2})/", path.replace("\\","/"))
    if m: return m.group(1)
    # default: most permissive for canon/meta
    return "N05"

def retrieve(query, k=3):
    # naive keyword retrieval over JSONL
    results = []
    q = query.lower().split()
    try:
        with open(INDEX_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            for line in f:
                rec = json.loads(line)
                text = rec["text"].lower()
                score = sum(text.count(tok) for tok in q)
                if score>0:
                    results.append((score, rec))
    except FileNotFoundError:
        return []
    results.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
    return [r[1] for r in results[:k]]

def ensure_index():
    if not os.path.exists(INDEX_PATH):
        rc, out = run(["python", "ai/index/build_index.py"])
        print(out)

def review_files(files):
    ensure_index()
    report = []
    for path in files:
        era = infer_era(path)
        report.append(f"### {path} (Era: {era})")
        # Lexicon lint
        rc, out = run(["python", LEX_LINT, path])
        if rc != 0:
            report.append("**Lexicon drift found:**")
            report.append("```")
            report.append(out.strip())
            report.append("```")
            # retrieve context
            recs = retrieve("Te’Oga time units lexicon")
            for r in recs:
                report.append(f"- See: `{r['path']}` (chunk {r['chunk_id']})")
        else:
            report.append("Lexicon: clean.")
        # Knowledge gate
        rc2, out2 = run(["python", KG_LINT, "--era", era, path])
        if rc2 != 0:
            report.append("**Knowledge Gate violations:**")
            report.append("```")
            report.append(out2.strip())
            report.append("```")
            recs = retrieve(f"{era} knowledge gates")
            for r in recs:
                report.append(f"- See: `{r['path']}` (chunk {r['chunk_id']})")
        else:
            report.append("Knowledge Gate: clean.")
        report.append("")
    return "\n".join(report)

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--base", default="origin/main")
    ap.add_argument("--head", default="HEAD")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default=os.environ.get("AI_REVIEW_OUT","ai_review_comment.md"))
    args = ap.parse_args()

    files = changed_files(args.base, args.head)
    body = ["# AI Review — Story Bible Enforcer", "", f"Files reviewed: {len(files)}", ""]
    body.append(review_files(files))
    text = "\n".join(body)

    # write comment body
    with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(text)
    print(f"Wrote review to {args.out}")
    print(text)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
"""
with open(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "ai_review.py"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(ai_review)

# Workflow to post PR comment
workflow = r"""name: AI Review

on:
  pull_request:
    types: [opened, synchronize, reopened]

jobs:
  ai-review:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: read
      pull-requests: write
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
        with:
          fetch-depth: 0
      - name: Set up Python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: '3.11'
      - name: Build index & run AI review
        run: |
          python ai/index/build_index.py
          python ai/ai_review.py --base origin/${{ github.base_ref }} --head ${{ github.sha }} --out /tmp/ai_review.md
      - name: Post PR comment
        uses: actions/github-script@v7
        with:
          script: |
            const fs = require('fs');
            const body = fs.readFileSync('/tmp/ai_review.md', 'utf8');
            await github.rest.issues.createComment({
              owner: context.repo.owner,
              repo: context.repo.repo,
              issue_number: context.issue.number,
              body
            });
"""
wf_path = os.path.join(ROOT, ".github", "workflows", "ai-review.yml")
with open(wf_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(workflow)

# Update top-level README with AI section
readme_path = os.path.join(ROOT, "README.md")
with open(readme_path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n\n## AI Assistant\n- RAG index + PR Review bot in `/ai`.\n- Action: `.github/workflows/ai-review.yml` posts automated reviews on PRs.\n- Local: `python ai/index/build_index.py && python ai/ai_review.py --base main --head HEAD`.\n")

# Re-zip repository for download
zip_path = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible.zip"
if os.path.exists(zip_path):
    os.remove(zip_path)
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
    for folder, _, files in os.walk(ROOT):
        for fn in files:
            full = os.path.join(folder, fn)
            z.write(full, os.path.relpath(full, ROOT))

print("AI scaffolding added. Zip updated.")
print(f"[ZIP] {zip_path}")

def copy_into(src_name, dest_relpath):
    src = f"/mnt/data/{src_name}"
    dst = os.path.join(ROOT, dest_relpath)
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(dst), exist_ok=True)
    if os.path.exists(src):
        shutil.copy2(src, dst)
        return True
    return False

# README for AI
readme_ai = """# AI Assistant (RAG + PR Review)

This folder gives you a minimal Retrieval-Augmented Generation setup and a **PR Review bot** that enforces canon, lexicon, and knowledge gates.

## Pieces
- `config.yaml` — what to index and how to chunk.
- `prompts/system.md` — system prompt + few-shots.
- `index/build_index.py` — creates `ai/index/index.jsonl` from `/docs`.
- `ai_review.py` — lints diffs, retrieves context from the index, and writes a PR comment.
- `tools/ai_stub.py` — optional LLM call wrapper (uses env vars).

## Local usage
```bash
python ai/index/build_index.py
python ai/ai_review.py --base main --head HEAD
```

## GitHub Action
`.github/workflows/ai-review.yml` runs on pull requests and posts an automated review comment.

## Secrets
- Add secrets in GitHub repo settings if you want model calls:
  - `OPENAI_API_KEY`  (or set locally in `.env`)
  - Optional: `OPENAI_BASE_URL`, `OPENAI_MODEL` (defaults sensible)
If not set, the bot still runs **rule-only** (linters + retrieval citations).
"""
write(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "README.md"), readme_ai)

# prompts/system.md
system_prompt = """You are **Story Bible Enforcer** for the Confluence Chronicles.

Hard rules:
- Obey Knowledge Gates per novella (N01–N30).
- Enforce Te’Oga lexicon (tide/anneal/crucible/casting; no modern time/tech vocabulary).
- Every working must show ≥1 cost (physio/psycho/systemic).
- Never invent canon; mark anything new as *Proposal* with justification.
- Cite repo paths (e.g., docs/01-canon/master-lexicon.md) when supporting a judgment.
- If unsure, request the minimal missing fact and continue with a best-effort, clearly labeled.

### Few-shot — Compliant Scene Ladder (N09)
- Era Gate: N09
- Knowledge: Confluence not named; Hollowing not medicalized.
- Beats:
  - Breach team rotates choir shield (Wholeness) for 6 breaths.
  - Jhace seats to Form, creates short-span braces; costs: tremor + after-heat.
  - Failure branch: lattice dust threatens cascade; breaker cuts link.
- Breath Budget: 4–8
- Costs: Physio + Systemic (vein-burn + fatigue)
- Aftermath FX: low hum, dust glow settles.

### Few-shot — Rejection + Fix
**Draft line:** "After an hour, they used Confluence to call the cops."
**Violations:** 'hour' (lexicon), 'Confluence' (N09 leak), 'cops' (lexicon).
**Fix:** "After two dozen breaths, they layered Form and Wholeness—no full chord—and signaled the guard cohort."
"""
write(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "prompts", "system.md"), system_prompt)

# index builder
indexer = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, re, argparse, glob, hashlib, yaml

def load_config(path):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return yaml.safe_load(f)

def read_text(path):
    try:
        return open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").read()
    except:
        return ""

def chunk_text(text, max_chars=1800, overlap=200):
    chunks = []
    start = 0
    n = len(text)
    while start < n:
        end = min(n, start + max_chars)
        cut = text.rfind("\n\n", start, end)
        if cut == -1 or cut <= start + 200:
            cut = end
        chunks.append(text[start:cut])
        start = max(cut - overlap, cut)
    return [c for c in chunks if c.strip()]

def path_tags(path):
    tags = []
    p = path.replace("\\", "/")
    m = re.search(r"/novellas/(N\d{2})", p)
    if m: tags.append(m.group(1))
    if "/01-canon/" in p: tags.append("canon")
    if "/05-ops/" in p: tags.append("ops")
    return tags

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--config", default="ai/config.yaml")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default="ai/index/index.jsonl")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    cfg = load_config(args.config)
    roots = cfg["index_roots"]
    patterns = cfg["file_globs"]
    max_chars = cfg["chunk"]["max_chars"]
    overlap = cfg["chunk"]["overlap"]

    records = []
    for root in roots:
        for pat in patterns:
            for path in glob.glob(os.path.join(root, pat), recursive=True):
                if not os.path.isfile(path): continue
                txt = read_text(path)
                for i, ch in enumerate(chunk_text(txt, max_chars, overlap)):
                    rid = hashlib.md5(f"{path}:{i}".encode()).hexdigest()
                    rec = {
                        "id": rid,
                        "path": path.replace("\\","/"),
                        "chunk_id": i,
                        "text": ch,
                        "tags": path_tags(path),
                    }
                    records.append(rec)

    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(args.out), exist_ok=True)
    with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for r in records:
            f.write(json.dumps(r, ensure_ascii=False)+"\n")
    print(f"Wrote {len(records)} chunks to {args.out}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
"""
write(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "index", "build_index.py"), indexer)

ai_review = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, subprocess, re, sys, argparse

REPO_ROOT = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), ".."))
LEX_LINT = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "tools", "lint", "lexicon_lint.py")

def run(cmd):
    p = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True)
    out,_ = p.communicate()
    return p.returncode, out

def changed_files(base, head):
    rc, out = run(["git", "diff", "--name-only", f"{base}...{head}"])
    paths = [l.strip() for l in out.splitlines() if l.strip()]
    md = [p for p in paths if p.endswith(('.md','.txt'))]
    if not md:
        for root, _, files in os.walk('docs'):
            for fn in files:
                if fn.endswith(('.md','.txt')):
                    md.append(os.path.join(root, fn))
    return sorted(set(md))

    m = re.search(r"/novellas/(N\d{2})/", path.replace('\\','/'))
    if m: return m.group(1)
    return "N05"

def ensure_index():
    if not os.path.exists(INDEX_PATH):
        rc, out = run(["python", "ai/index/build_index.py"])
        print(out)

def review_files(files):
    ensure_index()
    report = []
    for path in files:
        era = infer_era(path)
        report.append(f"### {path} (Era: {era})")
        rc, out = run(["python", LEX_LINT, path])
        if rc != 0:
            report.append("**Lexicon drift found:**\n```")
            report.append(out.strip())
            report.append("```\n")
        else:
            report.append("Lexicon: clean.\n")
        rc2, out2 = run(["python", KG_LINT, "--era", era, path])
        if rc2 != 0:
            report.append("**Knowledge Gate violations:**\n```")
            report.append(out2.strip())
            report.append("```\n")
        else:
            report.append("Knowledge Gate: clean.\n")
    return "\n".join(report)

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--base", default="origin/main")
    ap.add_argument("--head", default="HEAD")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default=os.environ.get("AI_REVIEW_OUT","ai_review_comment.md"))
    args = ap.parse_args()

    files = changed_files(args.base, args.head)
    header = "# AI Review — Story Bible Enforcer\n"
    body = header + f"\nFiles reviewed: {len(files)}\n\n" + review_files(files) + "\n"
    with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(body)
    print(f"Wrote review to {args.out}")
    print(body)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
"""
write(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "ai_review.py"), ai_review)

# Ingest the uploaded repo, add /ai RAG + PR-review scaffolding, update README, and re-zip.
import os, zipfile, shutil, json, textwrap, glob, re

UPLOAD_ZIP = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible (1).zip"

# Detect repo root (folder containing 'docs' or '.github')
def find_repo_root(base):
    # 1) if base directly contains docs, treat as root
    if os.path.isdir(os.path.join(base, "docs")) or os.path.isdir(os.path.join(base, ".github")):
        return base
    # 2) else look one level deep
    for name in os.listdir(base):
        p = os.path.join(base, name)
        if os.path.isdir(p) and (os.path.isdir(os.path.join(p, "docs")) or os.path.isdir(os.path.join(p, ".github"))):
            return p
    # 3) fallback: first directory
    for name in os.listdir(base):
        p = os.path.join(base, name)
        if os.path.isdir(p):
            return p
    return base

REPO_ROOT = find_repo_root(EXTRACT_ROOT)

def write(path, content):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(content.rstrip()+"\n")

### Few-shot — Compliant Scene Ladder (N09)

### Few-shot — Rejection + Fix

**Violations:** 'hour' (lexicon), 'Confluence' (N09 leak), 'cops' (lexicon).

# index/build_index.py (pure stdlib)
indexer = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, re, argparse, glob, hashlib

def read_text(path):
    try:
        return open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").read()
    except:
        return ""

def chunk_text(text, max_chars=1800, overlap=200):
    chunks = []
    start = 0
    n = len(text)
    while start < n:
        end = min(n, start + max_chars)
        cut = text.rfind("\n\n", start, end)
        if cut == -1 or cut <= start + 200:
            cut = end
        chunks.append(text[start:cut])
        start = max(cut - overlap, cut)
    return [c for c in chunks if c.strip()]

def path_tags(path):
    tags = []
    p = path.replace("\\", "/")
    m = re.search(r"/novellas/(N\d{2})", p)
    if m: tags.append(m.group(1))
    if "/01-canon/" in p: tags.append("canon")
    if "/05-ops/" in p: tags.append("ops")
    return tags

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--config", default="ai/config.json")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default="ai/index/index.jsonl")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    cfg = json.load(open(args.config, "r", encoding="utf-8"))
    roots = cfg["index_roots"]
    patterns = cfg["file_globs"]
    max_chars = cfg["chunk"]["max_chars"]
    overlap = cfg["chunk"]["overlap"]

    records = []
    for root in roots:
        for pat in patterns:
            for path in glob.glob(os.path.join(root, pat), recursive=True):
                if not os.path.isfile(path): continue
                txt = read_text(path)
                for i, ch in enumerate(chunk_text(txt, max_chars, overlap)):
                    rid = hashlib.md5(f"{path}:{i}".encode()).hexdigest()
                    rec = {
                        "id": rid,
                        "path": path.replace("\\","/"),
                        "chunk_id": i,
                        "text": ch,
                        "tags": path_tags(path),
                    }
                    records.append(rec)

    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(args.out), exist_ok=True)
    with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for r in records:
            f.write(json.dumps(r, ensure_ascii=False)+"\n")
    print(f"Wrote {len(records)} chunks to {args.out}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
"""
write(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "index", "build_index.py"), indexer)

"""

# ai_review.py
ai_review = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, subprocess, re, sys, argparse

REPO_ROOT = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), ".."))
LEX_LINT = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "tools", "lint", "lexicon_lint.py")
KG_LINT = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "tools", "lint", "knowledge_gate_lint.py")
INDEX_PATH = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "ai", "index", "index.jsonl")

def run(cmd):
    p = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True)
    out,_ = p.communicate()
    return p.returncode, out

def changed_files(base, head):
    rc, out = run(["git", "diff", "--name-only", f"{base}...{head}"])
    paths = [l.strip() for l in out.splitlines() if l.strip()]
    md = [p for p in paths if p.endswith(('.md','.txt'))]
    if not md:
        for root, _, files in os.walk('docs'):
            for fn in files:
                if fn.endswith(('.md','.txt')):
                    md.append(os.path.join(root, fn))
    return sorted(set(md))

def infer_era(path):
    m = re.search(r"/novellas/(N\d{2})/", path.replace('\\','/'))
    if m: return m.group(1)
    return "N05"

def ensure_index():
    if not os.path.exists(INDEX_PATH):
        rc, out = run(["python", "ai/index/build_index.py"])
        print(out)

def review_files(files):
    ensure_index()
    report = []
    for path in files:
        era = infer_era(path)
        report.append(f"### {path} (Era: {era})")
        # Lexicon
        if os.path.exists(LEX_LINT):
            rc, out = run(["python", LEX_LINT, path])
            if rc != 0:
                report.append("**Lexicon drift found:**\n```")
                report.append(out.strip())
                report.append("```\n")
            else:
                report.append("Lexicon: clean.\n")
        else:
            report.append("Lexicon linter not found.\n")
        # Knowledge gate
        if os.path.exists(KG_LINT):
            rc2, out2 = run(["python", KG_LINT, "--era", era, path])
            if rc2 != 0:
                report.append("**Knowledge Gate violations:**\n```")
                report.append(out2.strip())
                report.append("```\n")
            else:
                report.append("Knowledge Gate: clean.\n")
        else:
            report.append("Knowledge Gate linter not found.\n")
    return "\n".join(report)

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--base", default="origin/main")
    ap.add_argument("--head", default="HEAD")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default=os.environ.get("AI_REVIEW_OUT","ai_review_comment.md"))
    args = ap.parse_args()

    files = changed_files(args.base, args.head)
    header = "# AI Review — Story Bible Enforcer\n"
    body = header + f"\nFiles reviewed: {len(files)}\n\n" + review_files(files) + "\n"
    with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(body)
    print(f"Wrote review to {args.out}")
    print(body)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
"""
write(os.path.join(AI_ROOT, "ai_review.py"), ai_review)

bash = textwrap.dedent("""\
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# Usage:
#   GH_OWNER=<your-github-username> REPO_NAME=ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible \
#   REPO_DIR="<path to extracted repo>" ./bootstrap_repo.sh
#
# If you have GitHub CLI (`gh`) logged in, this will create the repo and push in one go.
# Otherwise, it prints the exact fallback git commands.

REPO_NAME="${REPO_NAME:-ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible}"
GH_OWNER="${GH_OWNER:-}"
REPO_DIR="${REPO_DIR:-$(pwd)}"
VISIBILITY="${VISIBILITY:---private}"   # --private | --public
DESCRIPTION="${DESCRIPTION:-Confluence Chronicles Story Bible + AI review tooling}"

if ! command -v git >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "git not found. Install git first."; exit 1
fi

if [[ -z "$GH_OWNER" ]]; then
  if command -v gh >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    GH_OWNER=$(gh api user --jq .login 2>/dev/null || echo "")
  fi
fi

cd "$REPO_DIR"

# Initialize repo if needed
if [ ! -d ".git" ]; then
  git init
  git add .
  git commit -m "Initial import: Story Bible + AI review"
  git branch -M main
fi

if command -v gh >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  # Create repo and push in one shot
  if [[ -n "$GH_OWNER" ]]; then
    gh repo create "$GH_OWNER/$REPO_NAME" $VISIBILITY --source "." --remote origin --push --description "$DESCRIPTION"
  else
    # Let gh prompt for owner
    gh repo create "$REPO_NAME" $VISIBILITY --source "." --remote origin --push --description "$DESCRIPTION"
  fi
else
  echo "GitHub CLI (gh) not found. Do it manually:"
  echo "1) Create a new repo named '$REPO_NAME' on GitHub (owner: $GH_OWNER)."
  echo "2) Then run:"
  echo "   git remote add origin git@github.com:$GH_OWNER/$REPO_NAME.git"
  echo "   git push -u origin main"
fi

echo ""

echo "- Open the 'Actions' tab; the 'AI Review' workflow should appear on PRs."

Short answer: I can’t push to your GitHub myself—I don’t have direct access to external accounts. But I just generated one-click bootstraps so you can create a brand-new repo and push everything in under a minute.

**Grab a script:**
- Bash (macOS/Linux): [bootstrap_repo.sh](sandbox:/mnt/data/bootstrap_repo.sh)  
- PowerShell (Windows): [bootstrap_repo.ps1](sandbox:/mnt/data/bootstrap_repo.ps1)

### Fast path (with GitHub CLI)
1. Install and log in: `gh auth login`
2. Extract the zip I gave you and set env vars, then run the script:

macOS/Linux:
```bash
export GH_OWNER=<your-github-username>
export REPO_NAME=ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible
export REPO_DIR="/path/to/extracted/repo"   # folder that has /docs, /ai, etc.
bash bootstrap_repo.sh
```

Windows PowerShell:
```powershell
$env:GH_OWNER="<your-github-username>"
$env:REPO_NAME="ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible"
$env:REPO_DIR="C:\Path\To\Extracted\Repo"
.\bootstrap_repo.ps1
```

The script will:
- `git init`, commit, set `main`
- Create a **new GitHub repo** via `gh repo create` (private by default)
- Push to `origin main`
- Remind you to enable Actions and (optionally) set AI secrets

### No GitHub CLI? Manual fallback
- Create an empty repo on GitHub named `ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible`
- In your extracted folder:
```bash
git init
git add .
git commit -m "Initial import: Story Bible + AI review"
git branch -M main
git remote add origin git@github.com:<you>/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible.git
git push -u origin main
```

### Optional: enable AI model calls
(Repo works fine without this; the PR bot still lints and cites canon.)
```bash
gh secret set OPENAI_API_KEY -b"YOUR_KEY"
gh secret set OPENAI_BASE_URL -b"https://api.openai.com/v1"   # optional
gh secret set OPENAI_MODEL -b"gpt-4o"                         # optional
```

Once it’s up, open a PR and you’ll see the **AI Review** workflow post its comments automatically. Ready for you to roll tape whenever.

def ensure_file(path, content):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(content.rstrip()+"\n")

def append_readme_note(root, note):
    readme = os.path.join(root, "README.md")
    try:
        txt = open(readme, "r", encoding="utf-8").read()
    except:
        txt = "# Confluence Chronicles — Story Bible\n"
    if note.strip() not in txt:
        with open(readme, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write("\n\n"+note.strip()+"\n")

# 5) Patch knowledge_gate_lint.py to accept N01..N30 (N06+ unlocked)
if os.path.isfile(kg_lint_py):
    txt = open(kg_lint_py, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").read()
    # Expand choices
    if "--era" in txt and "choices=" in txt and "N05" in txt and "N06" not in txt:
        txt = re.sub(r'choices=\[(.*?)\]', 'choices=[%s]' % ",".join([f'"N{n:02d}"' for n in range(1,31)]), txt, count=1, flags=re.S)
        # Expand BANS table to include N06..N30 as None
        if "BANS = {" in txt and "N05" in txt and "N06" not in txt:
            insert = ",\n" + ",\n".join([f'    "N{n:02d}": None' for n in range(6,31)]) + "\n}"
            txt = re.sub(r'\}\s*$', insert, txt, count=1, flags=re.S)
        with open(kg_lint_py, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write(txt)
else:
    # Create a permissive linter as fallback
    kg_code = textwrap.dedent("""\
    #!/usr/bin/env python3
    import sys, os, re, argparse

    BANS = {
        "N01": re.compile(r"\\b(resonance|principle|veins?|Hollowing|Confluence|suppression|factions?|god-?vessels?)\\b", re.I),
        "N02": re.compile(r"\\b(four principles|Hollowing|dual-?principle|Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\\b", re.I),
        "N03": re.compile(r"\\b(four principles|Hollowing|dual-?principle|Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\\b", re.I),
        "N04": re.compile(r"\\b(Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\\b", re.I),
    }
    for i in range(5,31):
        BANS[f"N{i:02d}"] = None

    def scan_file(path, era):
        rx = BANS.get(era)
        if not rx: return []
        try: txt = open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").read()
        except: return []
        hits = []
        for m in rx.finditer(txt):
            start = max(0, m.start()-40)
            end = min(len(txt), m.end()+40)
            ctx = txt[start:end].replace("\\n"," ")
            hits.append((m.group(0), ctx))
        return hits

    def main():
        ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Knowledge Gate linter")
        eras = [f"N{i:02d}" for i in range(1,31)]
        ap.add_argument("--era", required=True, choices=eras)
        ap.add_argument("paths", nargs="+")
        args = ap.parse_args()

        files = []
        for p in args.paths:
            if os.path.isdir(p):
                for root, _, fs in os.walk(p):
                    for fn in fs:
                        if fn.lower().endswith((".md",".markdown",".txt")):
                            files.append(os.path.join(root, fn))
            else:
                files.append(p)

        any_hits = False
        for f in sorted(files):
            hits = scan_file(f, args.era)
            for term, ctx in hits:
                any_hits = True
                print(f"[GATE {args.era}] {f}: term '{term}' not allowed")
                print(f"  ...{ctx}...")
        if any_hits:
            print(f"\\nKnowledge Gate {args.era} violations found.")
            sys.exit(1)
        else:
            print(f"Knowledge Gate {args.era}: clean.")
            sys.exit(0)

    if __name__ == "__main__":
        main()
    """)
    os.makedirs(tools_lint, exist_ok=True)
    ensure_file(kg_lint_py, kg_code)

# 6) Ensure CI workflows exist
wf_dir = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, ".github", "workflows")
os.makedirs(wf_dir, exist_ok=True)
ci_yml = os.path.join(wf_dir, "ci.yml")

# Step A: Unzip the uploaded repo and locate the root
import os, zipfile, shutil

UPLOAD_ZIP = "/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible (1).zip"
EXTRACT_ROOT = "/mnt/data/_repo_validate"

# Fresh extract
if os.path.exists(EXTRACT_ROOT):
    shutil.rmtree(EXTRACT_ROOT)
os.makedirs(EXTRACT_ROOT, exist_ok=True)

with zipfile.ZipFile(UPLOAD_ZIP, "r") as z:
    z.extractall(EXTRACT_ROOT)

def find_repo_root(base):
    # if base directly contains docs or .github, assume root
    if os.path.isdir(os.path.join(base, "docs")) or os.path.isdir(os.path.join(base, ".github")):
        return base
    # otherwise search one level deep
    for name in os.listdir(base):
        p = os.path.join(base, name)
        if os.path.isdir(p) and (os.path.isdir(os.path.join(p, "docs")) or os.path.isdir(os.path.join(p, ".github"))):
            return p
    # fallback: first dir
    for name in os.listdir(base):
        p = os.path.join(base, name)
        if os.path.isdir(p):
            return p
    return base

REPO_ROOT = find_repo_root(EXTRACT_ROOT)
print("REPO_ROOT:", REPO_ROOT)
print("Top-level entries:", sorted(os.listdir(REPO_ROOT))[:50])

# Step C: Fill gaps — scaffold N06–N30 ladders/chapters, ops decks N16–N30, ensure AI folder & workflows, patch knowledge linter
import os, textwrap, glob, shutil, re, json

REPO_ROOT = "/mnt/data/_repo_validate"

def write(path, content):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(content.rstrip()+"\n")

# 1) Scaffold novellas N06–N30 if missing
novellas_root = os.path.join(REPO_ROOT, "docs", "04-plot", "novellas")
os.makedirs(novellas_root, exist_ok=True)

def chapter_template(n):
    if 6 <= n <= 10:
        tier="Structured Beats (8–12)"
    elif 11 <= n <= 15:
        tier="Decision Trees"
    elif 16 <= n <= 20:
        tier="Ops-Backed Ladders"
    elif 21 <= n <= 25:
        tier="Timestamped Ladders"
    else:
        tier="Final Ops Decks"
    return textwrap.dedent(f"""
    # Chapter Ladder — N{n:02d}

    **Tier:** {tier}

    **Header (Te’Oga):**
    `Striketide • Ember Anneal • Final Temper • Casting ____ — Location`
    `d/a/c/____ — Location`

    ## Beats
    - [ ] ...
    """)

def ladder_doc(n, tier):
    return textwrap.dedent(f"""
    # Novella Ladder — N{n:02d}

    **Tier:** {tier}

    ## Knowledge & Continuity
    - Inherits N01–N05 canon (terms unlocked after N05). Maintain POV limits.
    - Costs are mandatory per working.

    ## Chapter List
    """ + "\n".join([f"- Ch{c:02d} —" for c in range(1,16)]))

for n in range(6,31):
    era_dir = os.path.join(novellas_root, f"N{n:02d}")
    ch_dir = os.path.join(era_dir, "chapters")
    if not os.path.isdir(era_dir):
        os.makedirs(ch_dir, exist_ok=True)
        # tier label
        if 6 <= n <= 10: tier="Tier A — Structured Beats"
        elif 11 <= n <= 15: tier="Tier B — Decision Trees"
        elif 16 <= n <= 20: tier="Tier C — Ops-Backed Ladders"
        elif 21 <= n <= 25: tier="Tier D — Timestamped Ladders"
        else: tier="Tier E — Final Ops Decks"
        write(os.path.join(era_dir, "ladder.md"), ladder_doc(n, tier))
        tpl = chapter_template(n)
        for c in range(1,16):
            write(os.path.join(ch_dir, f"Ch{c:02d}.md"), tpl)
    else:
        # ensure ladder and 15 chapters exist
        if not os.path.isfile(os.path.join(era_dir, "ladder.md")):
            if 6 <= n <= 10: tier="Tier A — Structured Beats"
            elif 11 <= n <= 15: tier="Tier B — Decision Trees"
            elif 16 <= n <= 20: tier="Tier C — Ops-Backed Ladders"
            elif 21 <= n <= 25: tier="Tier D — Timestamped Ladders"
            else: tier="Tier E — Final Ops Decks"
            write(os.path.join(era_dir, "ladder.md"), ladder_doc(n, tier))
        ch_dir = os.path.join(era_dir, "chapters")
        os.makedirs(ch_dir, exist_ok=True)
        for c in range(1,16):
            pth = os.path.join(ch_dir, f"Ch{c:02d}.md")
            if not os.path.isfile(pth):
                write(pth, chapter_template(n))

# 2) Scaffold ops decks N16–N30 if missing

    #!/usr/bin/env python3
    import sys, re, os, argparse
    SUB = [(re.compile(r"\\bweeks?\\b", re.I),"anneal/anneals")]
    def scan(p):
        try: t=open(p,"r",encoding="utf-8",errors="ignore").read()
        except: return []
        hits=[]
        for rx,rep in SUB:
            for m in rx.finditer(t):
                hits.append((p,m.group(0),rep))
        return hits
    def main():
        ap=argparse.ArgumentParser(); ap.add_argument("paths",nargs="+"); a=ap.parse_args()
        files=[]
        for p in a.paths:
            if os.path.isdir(p):

                print(f"[LEXICON] {path}: '{term}' -> '{rep}'"); bad=True
        print("Lexicon linter: {}.".format("violations" if bad else "clean"))
        sys.exit(1 if bad else 0)
    if __name__=="__main__": main()
    """))

        "N04": re.compile(r"\\b(Confluence|suppression|god-?vessels?)\\b", re.I),
